122: // 3D Simplex Noise
123: float snoise(vec3 v) {
124:   const vec2  C = vec2(1.0/6.0, 1.0/3.0) ;
125:   const vec4  D = vec4(0.0, 0.5, 1.0, 2.0);
126: 
127:   // First corner
128:   vec3 i  = floor(v + dot(v, C.yyy) );
129:   vec3 x0 =   v - i + dot(i, C.xxx) ;
130: 
131:   // Other corners
132:   vec3 g = step(x0.yzx, x0.xyz);
133:   vec3 l = 1.0 - g;
134:   vec3 i1 = min( g.xyz, l.zxy );
135:   vec3 i2 = max( g.xyz, l.zxy );
136: 
137:   vec3 x1 = x0 - i1 + C.xxx;
138:   vec3 x2 = x0 - i2 + C.yyy;
139:   vec3 x3 = x0 - D.yyy;
140: 
141:   // Permutations
142:   vec4 p = permute( permute( permute(
143:             i.z + vec4(0.0, i1.z, i2.z, 1.0 ))
144:           + i.y + vec4(0.0, i1.y, i2.y, 1.0 ))
145:           + i.x + vec4(0.0, i1.x, i2.x, 1.0 ));
146: 
147:   // Gradients
148:   float n_ = 0.142857142857; // 1.0/7.0
149:   vec3  ns = n_ * D.wyz - D.xzx;
150: 
151:   vec4 j = p - 49.0 * floor(p * ns.z * ns.z);
152: 
153:   vec4 x_ = floor(j * ns.z);
154:   vec4 y_ = floor(j - 7.0 * x_ );
155: 
156:   vec4 x = x_ *ns.x + ns.yyyy;
157:   vec4 y = y_ *ns.x + ns.yyyy;
158:   vec4 h = 1.0 - abs(x) - abs(y);
159: 
160:   vec4 b0 = vec4( x.xy, y.xy );
161:   vec4 b1 = vec4( x.zw, y.zw );
162: 
163:   vec4 s0 = floor(b0)*2.0 + 1.0;
164:   vec4 s1 = floor(b1)*2.0 + 1.0;
165:   vec4 sh = -step(h, vec4(0.0));
166: 
167:   vec4 a0 = b0.xzyw + s0.xzyw*sh.xxyy ;
168:   vec4 a1 = b1.xzyw + s1.xzyw*sh.zzww ;
169: 
170:   vec3 p0 = vec3(a0.xy,h.x);
171:   vec3 p1 = vec3(a0.zw,h.y);
172:   vec3 p2 = vec3(a1.xy,h.z);
173:   vec3 p3 = vec3(a1.zw,h.w);
174: 
175:   // Normalise gradients
176:   vec4 norm = taylorInvSqrt(vec4(dot(p0,p0), dot(p1,p1), dot(p2, p2), dot(p3,p3)));
177:   p0 *= norm.x;
178:   p1 *= norm.y;
179:   p2 *= norm.z;
180:   p3 *= norm.w;
181: 
182:   // Mix final noise value
183:   vec4 m = max(0.6 - vec4(dot(x0,x0), dot(x1,x1), dot(x2,x2), dot(x3,x3)), 0.0);
184:   m = m * m;
185:   return 42.0 * dot( m*m, vec4( dot(p0,x0), dot(p1,x1),
186:                                 dot(p2,x2), dot(p3,x3) ) );
187: }
188: 
189: // Classic Perlin noise
190: float cnoise(vec3 P)
191: {
192:   vec3 Pi0 = floor(P); 
193:   vec3 Pi1 = Pi0 + vec3(1.0); 
194:   
195:   vec3 Pf0 = fract(P); 
196:   vec3 Pf1 = Pf0 - vec3(1.0); 
197:   vec4 ix = vec4(Pi0.x, Pi1.x, Pi0.x, Pi1.x);
198:   vec4 iy = vec4(Pi0.yy, Pi1.yy);
199:   vec4 iz0 = Pi0.zzzz;
200:   vec4 iz1 = Pi1.zzzz;
201: 
202:   vec4 ixy = permute(permute(ix) + iy);
203:   vec4 ixy0 = permute(ixy + iz0);
204:   vec4 ixy1 = permute(ixy + iz1);
205: 
206:   vec4 gx0 = ixy0 * (1.0 / 7.0);
207:   vec4 gy0 = fract(floor(gx0) * (1.0 / 7.0)) - 0.5;
208:   gx0 = fract(gx0);
209:   vec4 gz0 = vec4(0.5) - abs(gx0) - abs(gy0);
210:   vec4 sz0 = step(gz0, vec4(0.0));
211:   gx0 -= sz0 * (step(0.0, gx0) - 0.5);
212:   gy0 -= sz0 * (step(0.0, gy0) - 0.5);
213: 
214:   vec4 gx1 = ixy1 * (1.0 / 7.0);
215:   vec4 gy1 = fract(floor(gx1) * (1.0 / 7.0)) - 0.5;
216:   gx1 = fract(gx1);
217:   vec4 gz1 = vec4(0.5) - abs(gx1) - abs(gy1);
218:   vec4 sz1 = step(gz1, vec4(0.0));
219:   gx1 -= sz1 * (step(0.0, gx1) - 0.5);
220:   gy1 -= sz1 * (step(0.0, gy1) - 0.5);
221: 
222:   vec3 g000 = vec3(gx0.x,gy0.x,gz0.x);
223:   vec3 g100 = vec3(gx0.y,gy0.y,gz0.y);
224:   vec3 g010 = vec3(gx0.z,gy0.z,gz0.z);
225:   vec3 g110 = vec3(gx0.w,gy0.w,gz0.w);
226:   vec3 g001 = vec3(gx1.x,gy1.x,gz1.x);
227:   vec3 g101 = vec3(gx1.y,gy1.y,gz1.y);
228:   vec3 g011 = vec3(gx1.z,gy1.z,gz1.z);
229:   vec3 g111 = vec3(gx1.w,gy1.w,gz1.w);
230: 
231:   vec4 norm0 = taylorInvSqrt(vec4(dot(g000, g000), dot(g010, g010), dot(g100, g100), dot(g110, g110)));
232:   g000 *= norm0.x;
233:   g010 *= norm0.y;
234:   g100 *= norm0.z;
235:   g110 *= norm0.w;
236:   vec4 norm1 = taylorInvSqrt(vec4(dot(g001, g001), dot(g011, g011), dot(g101, g101), dot(g111, g111)));
237:   g001 *= norm1.x;
238:   g011 *= norm1.y;
239:   g101 *= norm1.z;
240:   g111 *= norm1.w;
241: 
242:   float n000 = dot(g000, Pf0);
243:   float n100 = dot(g100, vec3(Pf1.x, Pf0.yz));
244:   float n010 = dot(g010, vec3(Pf0.x, Pf1.y, Pf0.z));
245:   float n110 = dot(g110, vec3(Pf1.xy, Pf0.z));
246:   float n001 = dot(g001, vec3(Pf0.xy, Pf1.z));
247:   float n101 = dot(g101, vec3(Pf1.x, Pf0.y, Pf1.z));
248:   float n011 = dot(g011, vec3(Pf0.x, Pf1.yz));
249:   float n111 = dot(g111, Pf1);
250: 
251:   vec3 fade_xyz = fade(Pf0);
252:   vec4 n_z = mix(vec4(n000, n100, n010, n110), vec4(n001, n101, n011, n111), fade_xyz.z);
253:   vec2 n_yz = mix(n_z.xy, n_z.zw, fade_xyz.y);
254:   float n_xyz = mix(n_yz.x, n_yz.y, fade_xyz.x);
255:   return 2.2 * n_xyz;
256: }
257: 
258: 
259: float random(vec2 p) {
260:     return fract(sin(dot(p, vec2(12.9898,78.233))) * 43758.5453);
261: }
262: 
263: float fbm(vec3 x) {
264:     float value = 0.0;
265:     float amplitude = 0.5;
266:     float frequency = 1.0;
267:     for (int i = 0; i < 4; i++) {
268:         value += amplitude * snoise(x * frequency);
269:         frequency *= 2.0;
270:         amplitude *= 0.5;
271:     }
272:     return value;
273: }
274: 
275: void main() {
276:     // MOUSE DISTORTION
277:     vec2 finalUv = vFlowUv;
278:     
279:     if (u_mouse_distortion_strength > 0.0) {
280:         vec4 mouseColor = texture2D(u_mouse_texture, vUv);
281:         float mouseValue = mouseColor.r;
282:         
283:         if (mouseValue > 0.001) {
284:             float distortionAmount = mouseValue * u_mouse_distortion_strength;
285:             vec2 mouseDisp = vec2(distortionAmount, distortionAmount);
286:             finalUv -= mouseDisp;
287:         }
288:     }
289:     
290:     vec3 baseColor;
291: 
292:     if (u_enable_procedural_texture > 0.5) {
293:         // Calculate flow field distance for ease effect
294:         vec2 ppp = -1.0 + 2.0 * finalUv;
295:         ppp += 0.1 * cos((1.5 * u_flow_scale) * ppp.yx + 1.1 * u_time + vec2(0.1, 1.1));
296:         ppp += 0.1 * cos((2.3 * u_flow_scale) * ppp.yx + 1.3 * u_time + vec2(3.2, 3.4));
297:         ppp += 0.1 * cos((2.2 * u_flow_scale) * ppp.yx + 1.7 * u_time + vec2(1.8, 5.2));
298:         ppp += u_flow_distortion_a * cos((u_flow_distortion_b * u_flow_scale) * ppp.yx + 1.4 * u_time + vec2(6.3, 3.9));
299:         float r = length(ppp); // Flow distance
300:         
301:         // Ease blending: 0 = topographic (flow), 1 = image (UV)
302:         float vx = (finalUv.x * u_texture_ease) + (r * (1.0 - u_texture_ease));
303:         float vy = (finalUv.y * u_texture_ease) + (0.0 * (1.0 - u_texture_ease));
304:         vec2 texUv = vec2(vx, vy);
305: 
306:         // PARALLAX SCROLLING
307:         // We manually apply a smaller offset here to make the texture lag behind
308:         float parallaxFactor = 0.25; // 25% speed of the color mixing
309:         texUv.y -= (u_y_offset * u_y_offset_color_multiplier / u_plane_height) * parallaxFactor;
310: 
311:         texUv *= 1.5; // Tiling scale
312: 
313:         vec4 texSample = texture2D(u_procedural_texture, texUv);
314:         baseColor = texSample.rgb;
315:     } else {
316:         baseColor = v_color;
317:     }
318: 
319:     vec3 color = baseColor;
320: 
321:     // Post-processing
322:     color += pow(v_displacement_amount, 1.0) * u_highlights;
323:     color -= pow(1.0 - v_displacement_amount, 2.0) * u_shadows;
324:     color = saturation(color, 1.0 + u_saturation);
325:     color = color * u_brightness;
326: 
327:     // Grain
328:     vec2 noiseCoords = gl_FragCoord.xy / u_grain_scale;
329:     float grain = (u_grain_speed != 0.0) ? fbm(vec3(noiseCoords, u_time * u_grain_speed)) : fbm(vec3(noiseCoords, 0.0));
330: 
331:     grain = grain * 0.5 + 0.5;
332:     grain -= 0.5;
333:     grain = (grain > u_grain_sparsity) ? grain : 0.0;
334:     grain *= u_grain_intensity;
335: 
336:     color += vec3(grain);
337: 
338:     gl_FragColor = vec4(color, 1.0);
339: }

75: // 3D Simplex Noise
76: float snoise(vec3 v) {
77:   const vec2  C = vec2(1.0/6.0, 1.0/3.0) ;
78:   const vec4  D = vec4(0.0, 0.5, 1.0, 2.0);
79: 
80:   // First corner
81:   vec3 i  = floor(v + dot(v, C.yyy) );
82:   vec3 x0 =   v - i + dot(i, C.xxx) ;
83: 
84:   // Other corners
85:   vec3 g = step(x0.yzx, x0.xyz);
86:   vec3 l = 1.0 - g;
87:   vec3 i1 = min( g.xyz, l.zxy );
88:   vec3 i2 = max( g.xyz, l.zxy );
89: 
90:   vec3 x1 = x0 - i1 + C.xxx;
91:   vec3 x2 = x0 - i2 + C.yyy;
92:   vec3 x3 = x0 - D.yyy;
93: 
94:   // Permutations
95:   vec4 p = permute( permute( permute(
96:             i.z + vec4(0.0, i1.z, i2.z, 1.0 ))
97:           + i.y + vec4(0.0, i1.y, i2.y, 1.0 ))
98:           + i.x + vec4(0.0, i1.x, i2.x, 1.0 ));
99: 
100:   // Gradients
101:   float n_ = 0.142857142857; // 1.0/7.0
102:   vec3  ns = n_ * D.wyz - D.xzx;
103: 
104:   vec4 j = p - 49.0 * floor(p * ns.z * ns.z);
105: 
106:   vec4 x_ = floor(j * ns.z);
107:   vec4 y_ = floor(j - 7.0 * x_ );
108: 
109:   vec4 x = x_ *ns.x + ns.yyyy;
110:   vec4 y = y_ *ns.x + ns.yyyy;
111:   vec4 h = 1.0 - abs(x) - abs(y);
112: 
113:   vec4 b0 = vec4( x.xy, y.xy );
114:   vec4 b1 = vec4( x.zw, y.zw );
115: 
116:   vec4 s0 = floor(b0)*2.0 + 1.0;
117:   vec4 s1 = floor(b1)*2.0 + 1.0;
118:   vec4 sh = -step(h, vec4(0.0));
119: 
120:   vec4 a0 = b0.xzyw + s0.xzyw*sh.xxyy ;
121:   vec4 a1 = b1.xzyw + s1.xzyw*sh.zzww ;
122: 
123:   vec3 p0 = vec3(a0.xy,h.x);
124:   vec3 p1 = vec3(a0.zw,h.y);
125:   vec3 p2 = vec3(a1.xy,h.z);
126:   vec3 p3 = vec3(a1.zw,h.w);
127: 
128:   // Normalise gradients
129:   vec4 norm = taylorInvSqrt(vec4(dot(p0,p0), dot(p1,p1), dot(p2, p2), dot(p3,p3)));
130:   p0 *= norm.x;
131:   p1 *= norm.y;
132:   p2 *= norm.z;
133:   p3 *= norm.w;
134: 
135:   // Mix final noise value
136:   vec4 m = max(0.6 - vec4(dot(x0,x0), dot(x1,x1), dot(x2,x2), dot(x3,x3)), 0.0);
137:   m = m * m;
138:   return 42.0 * dot( m*m, vec4( dot(p0,x0), dot(p1,x1),
139:                                 dot(p2,x2), dot(p3,x3) ) );
140: }
141: 
142: // Classic Perlin noise
143: float cnoise(vec3 P)
144: {
145:   vec3 Pi0 = floor(P); 
146:   vec3 Pi1 = Pi0 + vec3(1.0); 
147:   
148:   vec3 Pf0 = fract(P); 
149:   vec3 Pf1 = Pf0 - vec3(1.0); 
150:   vec4 ix = vec4(Pi0.x, Pi1.x, Pi0.x, Pi1.x);
151:   vec4 iy = vec4(Pi0.yy, Pi1.yy);
152:   vec4 iz0 = Pi0.zzzz;
153:   vec4 iz1 = Pi1.zzzz;
154: 
155:   vec4 ixy = permute(permute(ix) + iy);
156:   vec4 ixy0 = permute(ixy + iz0);
157:   vec4 ixy1 = permute(ixy + iz1);
158: 
159:   vec4 gx0 = ixy0 * (1.0 / 7.0);
160:   vec4 gy0 = fract(floor(gx0) * (1.0 / 7.0)) - 0.5;
161:   gx0 = fract(gx0);
162:   vec4 gz0 = vec4(0.5) - abs(gx0) - abs(gy0);
163:   vec4 sz0 = step(gz0, vec4(0.0));
164:   gx0 -= sz0 * (step(0.0, gx0) - 0.5);
165:   gy0 -= sz0 * (step(0.0, gy0) - 0.5);
166: 
167:   vec4 gx1 = ixy1 * (1.0 / 7.0);
168:   vec4 gy1 = fract(floor(gx1) * (1.0 / 7.0)) - 0.5;
169:   gx1 = fract(gx1);
170:   vec4 gz1 = vec4(0.5) - abs(gx1) - abs(gy1);
171:   vec4 sz1 = step(gz1, vec4(0.0));
172:   gx1 -= sz1 * (step(0.0, gx1) - 0.5);
173:   gy1 -= sz1 * (step(0.0, gy1) - 0.5);
174: 
175:   vec3 g000 = vec3(gx0.x,gy0.x,gz0.x);
176:   vec3 g100 = vec3(gx0.y,gy0.y,gz0.y);
177:   vec3 g010 = vec3(gx0.z,gy0.z,gz0.z);
178:   vec3 g110 = vec3(gx0.w,gy0.w,gz0.w);
179:   vec3 g001 = vec3(gx1.x,gy1.x,gz1.x);
180:   vec3 g101 = vec3(gx1.y,gy1.y,gz1.y);
181:   vec3 g011 = vec3(gx1.z,gy1.z,gz1.z);
182:   vec3 g111 = vec3(gx1.w,gy1.w,gz1.w);
183: 
184:   vec4 norm0 = taylorInvSqrt(vec4(dot(g000, g000), dot(g010, g010), dot(g100, g100), dot(g110, g110)));
185:   g000 *= norm0.x;
186:   g010 *= norm0.y;
187:   g100 *= norm0.z;
188:   g110 *= norm0.w;
189:   vec4 norm1 = taylorInvSqrt(vec4(dot(g001, g001), dot(g011, g011), dot(g101, g101), dot(g111, g111)));
190:   g001 *= norm1.x;
191:   g011 *= norm1.y;
192:   g101 *= norm1.z;
193:   g111 *= norm1.w;
194: 
195:   float n000 = dot(g000, Pf0);
196:   float n100 = dot(g100, vec3(Pf1.x, Pf0.yz));
197:   float n010 = dot(g010, vec3(Pf0.x, Pf1.y, Pf0.z));
198:   float n110 = dot(g110, vec3(Pf1.xy, Pf0.z));
199:   float n001 = dot(g001, vec3(Pf0.xy, Pf1.z));
200:   float n101 = dot(g101, vec3(Pf1.x, Pf0.y, Pf1.z));
201:   float n011 = dot(g011, vec3(Pf0.x, Pf1.yz));
202:   float n111 = dot(g111, Pf1);
203: 
204:   vec3 fade_xyz = fade(Pf0);
205:   vec4 n_z = mix(vec4(n000, n100, n010, n110), vec4(n001, n101, n011, n111), fade_xyz.z);
206:   vec2 n_yz = mix(n_z.xy, n_z.zw, fade_xyz.y);
207:   float n_xyz = mix(n_yz.x, n_yz.y, fade_xyz.x);
208:   return 2.2 * n_xyz;
209: }
210: 
211: vec3 saturation(vec3 rgb, float adjustment) {
212:     const vec3 W = vec3(0.2125, 0.7154, 0.0721);
213:     vec3 intensity = vec3(dot(rgb, W));
214:     return mix(intensity, rgb, adjustment);
215: }
216: 
217: float get_saturation(vec3 rgb)
218: {
219:     vec4 K = vec4(0.0, -1.0 / 3.0, 2.0 / 3.0, -1.0);
220:     vec4 p = mix(vec4(rgb.bg, K.wz), vec4(rgb.gb, K.xy), step(rgb.b, rgb.g));
221:     vec4 q = mix(vec4(p.xyw, rgb.r), vec4(rgb.r, p.yzx), step(p.x, rgb.r));
222: 
223:     float d = q.x - min(q.w, q.y);
224:     float e = 1.0e-10;
225:     return abs(6.0 * d + e);
226: }
227: 
228: // get saturation of a color in values between 0 and 1
229: float getSaturationMix(vec3 color) {
230:     float max = max(color.r, max(color.g, color.b));
231:     float min = min(color.r, min(color.g, color.b));
232:     return (max - min) / max;
233: }
234:     
235: vec3 rgb2hsv(vec3 c)
236: {
237:     vec4 K = vec4(0.0, -1.0 / 3.0, 2.0 / 3.0, -1.0);
238:     vec4 p = mix(vec4(c.bg, K.wz), vec4(c.gb, K.xy), step(c.b, c.g));
239:     vec4 q = mix(vec4(p.xyw, c.r), vec4(c.r, p.yzx), step(p.x, c.r));
240: 
241:     float d = q.x - min(q.w, q.y);
242:     float e = 1.0e-10;
243:     return vec3(abs(q.z + (q.w - q.y) / (6.0 * d + e)), d / (q.x + e), q.x);
244: }
245: 
246: vec3 hsv2rgb(vec3 c)
247: {
248:     vec4 K = vec4(1.0, 2.0 / 3.0, 1.0 / 3.0, 3.0);
249:     vec3 p = abs(fract(c.xxx + K.xyz) * 6.0 - K.www);
250:     return c.z * mix(K.xxx, clamp(p - K.xxx, 0.0, 1.0), c.y);
251: }
252: 
253: // Color related helper functions
254: vec3 blendColors(vec3 colorA, vec3 colorB, float weight) {
255:     return mix(colorA, colorB, weight);
256: }

258: precision highp float;
259: 
260: attribute vec3 position;
261: attribute vec3 normal;
262: attribute vec2 uv;
263: 
264: uniform mat4 modelViewMatrix;
265: uniform mat4 projectionMatrix;
266: 
267: // Uniforms injected by THREE previously:
268: // NONE that we don't define manually here.
269: 
270: void main() {
271:     vUv = uv;
272: 
273:     // SCROLLING LOGIC
274:     // Separate multipliers for wave, color, and flow offsets
275:     float waveOffset = -u_y_offset * u_y_offset_wave_multiplier;
276:     float colorOffset = -u_y_offset * u_y_offset_color_multiplier;
277:     float flowOffset = -u_y_offset * u_y_offset_flow_multiplier;
278: 
279:     // 1. DISPLACEMENT (WAVES)
280:     // We add waveOffset to Y to scroll the wave pattern
281:     v_displacement_amount = cnoise( vec3(
282:         u_wave_frequency_x * position.x + u_time,
283:         u_wave_frequency_y * (position.y + waveOffset) + u_time,
284:         u_time
285:     ));
286: 
287:     // 2. FLOW FIELD
288:     // Apply flow offset to scroll the flow field mask
289:     vec2 baseUv = vUv;
290:     baseUv.y += flowOffset / u_plane_height; // Scale to match wave speed
291:     vec2 flowUv = baseUv;
292: 
293:     if (u_flow_enabled > 0.5) {
294:         if (u_flow_ease > 0.0 || u_flow_distortion_a > 0.0) {
295:             vec2 ppp = -1.0 + 2.0 * baseUv;
296:             ppp += 0.1 * cos((1.5 * u_flow_scale) * ppp.yx + 1.1 * u_time + vec2(0.1, 1.1));
297:             ppp += 0.1 * cos((2.3 * u_flow_scale) * ppp.yx + 1.3 * u_time + vec2(3.2, 3.4));
298:             ppp += 0.1 * cos((2.2 * u_flow_scale) * ppp.yx + 1.7 * u_time + vec2(1.8, 5.2));
299:             ppp += u_flow_distortion_a * cos((u_flow_distortion_b * u_flow_scale) * ppp.yx + 1.4 * u_time + vec2(6.3, 3.9));
300: 
301:             float r = length(ppp);
302:             flowUv = mix(baseUv, vec2(baseUv.x * (1.0 - u_flow_ease) + r * u_flow_ease, baseUv.y), u_flow_ease);
303:         }
304:     }
305: 
306:     // Pass the standard flow UV to fragment shader (for mouse/texture)
307:     vFlowUv = flowUv;
308: 
309:     // 3. COLOR MIXING
310:     // We take the computed flow UVs and apply the color offset
311:     // Scale by plane height to match wave offset speed (world space vs UV space)
312:     vec3 color = u_colors[0].color;
313:     // ...
314:     vec2 adjustedUv = flowUv;
315:     adjustedUv.y += colorOffset / u_plane_height; // Scroll the color mixing pattern
316: 
317:     vec2 noise_cord = adjustedUv * u_color_pressure;
318:     const float minNoise = .0;
319:     const float maxNoise = .9;
320: 
321:     for (int i = 1; i < 6; i++) {
322:         if(i >= u_colors_count) break;
323:         if(u_colors[i].is_active > 0.5){
324:             float noiseFlow = (1. + float(i)) / 30.;
325:             float noiseSpeed = (1. + float(i)) * 0.11;
326:             float noiseSeed = 13. + float(i) * 7.;
327: 
328:             float noise = snoise(
329:                 vec3(
330:                     noise_cord.x * u_color_pressure.x + u_time * noiseFlow * 2.,
331:                     noise_cord.y * u_color_pressure.y,
332:                     u_time * noiseSpeed
333:                 ) + noiseSeed
334:             ) - (.1 * float(i)) + (.5 * u_color_blending);
335: 
336:             noise = clamp(minNoise, maxNoise + float(i) * 0.02, noise);
337:             color = mix(color, u_colors[i].color, smoothstep(0.0, u_color_blending, noise));
338:         }
339:     }
340: 
341:     v_color = color;
342: 
343:     // 4. VERTEX POSITION
344:     vec3 newPosition = position + normal * v_displacement_amount * u_wave_amplitude;
345:     gl_Position = projectionMatrix * modelViewMatrix * vec4(newPosition, 1.0);
346:     v_new_position = gl_Position;
347: }

106: // 1. REPLACEMENT PERMUTE: 
107: // Uses a hash function (fract/sin) instead of a modular lookup table.
108: vec4 permute(vec4 x) {
109:     return floor(fract(sin(x) * 43758.5453123) * 289.0);
110: }
111: 
112: // Taylor Inverse Sqrt
113: vec4 taylorInvSqrt(vec4 r) {
114:   return 1.79284291400159 - 0.85373472095314 * r;
115: }
116: 
117: // Fade function
118: vec3 fade(vec3 t) {
119:   return t*t*t*(t*(t*6.0-15.0)+10.0);
120: }
121: 
122: // 3D Simplex Noise
123: float snoise(vec3 v) {
124:   const vec2  C = vec2(1.0/6.0, 1.0/3.0) ;
125:   const vec4  D = vec4(0.0, 0.5, 1.0, 2.0);
126: 
127:   // First corner
128:   vec3 i  = floor(v + dot(v, C.yyy) );
129:   vec3 x0 =   v - i + dot(i, C.xxx) ;
130: 
131:   // Other corners
132:   vec3 g = step(x0.yzx, x0.xyz);
133:   vec3 l = 1.0 - g;
134:   vec3 i1 = min( g.xyz, l.zxy );
135:   vec3 i2 = max( g.xyz, l.zxy );
136: 
137:   vec3 x1 = x0 - i1 + C.xxx;
138:   vec3 x2 = x0 - i2 + C.yyy;
139:   vec3 x3 = x0 - D.yyy;
140: 
141:   // Permutations
142:   vec4 p = permute( permute( permute(
143:             i.z + vec4(0.0, i1.z, i2.z, 1.0 ))
144:           + i.y + vec4(0.0, i1.y, i2.y, 1.0 ))
145:           + i.x + vec4(0.0, i1.x, i2.x, 1.0 ));
146: 
147:   // Gradients
148:   float n_ = 0.142857142857; // 1.0/7.0
149:   vec3  ns = n_ * D.wyz - D.xzx;
150: 
151:   vec4 j = p - 49.0 * floor(p * ns.z * ns.z);
152: 
153:   vec4 x_ = floor(j * ns.z);
154:   vec4 y_ = floor(j - 7.0 * x_ );
155: 
156:   vec4 x = x_ *ns.x + ns.yyyy;
157:   vec4 y = y_ *ns.x + ns.yyyy;
158:   vec4 h = 1.0 - abs(x) - abs(y);
159: 
160:   vec4 b0 = vec4( x.xy, y.xy );
161:   vec4 b1 = vec4( x.zw, y.zw );
162: 
163:   vec4 s0 = floor(b0)*2.0 + 1.0;
164:   vec4 s1 = floor(b1)*2.0 + 1.0;
165:   vec4 sh = -step(h, vec4(0.0));
166: 
167:   vec4 a0 = b0.xzyw + s0.xzyw*sh.xxyy ;
168:   vec4 a1 = b1.xzyw + s1.xzyw*sh.zzww ;
169: 
170:   vec3 p0 = vec3(a0.xy,h.x);
171:   vec3 p1 = vec3(a0.zw,h.y);
172:   vec3 p2 = vec3(a1.xy,h.z);
173:   vec3 p3 = vec3(a1.zw,h.w);
174: 
175:   // Normalise gradients
176:   vec4 norm = taylorInvSqrt(vec4(dot(p0,p0), dot(p1,p1), dot(p2, p2), dot(p3,p3)));
177:   p0 *= norm.x;
178:   p1 *= norm.y;
179:   p2 *= norm.z;
180:   p3 *= norm.w;
181: 
182:   // Mix final noise value
183:   vec4 m = max(0.6 - vec4(dot(x0,x0), dot(x1,x1), dot(x2,x2), dot(x3,x3)), 0.0);
184:   m = m * m;
185:   return 42.0 * dot( m*m, vec4( dot(p0,x0), dot(p1,x1),
186:                                 dot(p2,x2), dot(p3,x3) ) );
187: }
188: 
189: // Classic Perlin noise
190: float cnoise(vec3 P)
191: {
192:   vec3 Pi0 = floor(P); 
193:   vec3 Pi1 = Pi0 + vec3(1.0); 
194:   
195:   vec3 Pf0 = fract(P); 
196:   vec3 Pf1 = Pf0 - vec3(1.0); 
197:   vec4 ix = vec4(Pi0.x, Pi1.x, Pi0.x, Pi1.x);
198:   vec4 iy = vec4(Pi0.yy, Pi1.yy);
199:   vec4 iz0 = Pi0.zzzz;
200:   vec4 iz1 = Pi1.zzzz;
201: 
202:   vec4 ixy = permute(permute(ix) + iy);
203:   vec4 ixy0 = permute(ixy + iz0);
204:   vec4 ixy1 = permute(ixy + iz1);
205: 
206:   vec4 gx0 = ixy0 * (1.0 / 7.0);
207:   vec4 gy0 = fract(floor(gx0) * (1.0 / 7.0)) - 0.5;
208:   gx0 = fract(gx0);
209:   vec4 gz0 = vec4(0.5) - abs(gx0) - abs(gy0);
210:   vec4 sz0 = step(gz0, vec4(0.0));
211:   gx0 -= sz0 * (step(0.0, gx0) - 0.5);
212:   gy0 -= sz0 * (step(0.0, gy0) - 0.5);
213: 
214:   vec4 gx1 = ixy1 * (1.0 / 7.0);
215:   vec4 gy1 = fract(floor(gx1) * (1.0 / 7.0)) - 0.5;
216:   gx1 = fract(gx1);
217:   vec4 gz1 = vec4(0.5) - abs(gx1) - abs(gy1);
218:   vec4 sz1 = step(gz1, vec4(0.0));
219:   gx1 -= sz1 * (step(0.0, gx1) - 0.5);
220:   gy1 -= sz1 * (step(0.0, gy1) - 0.5);
221: 
222:   vec3 g000 = vec3(gx0.x,gy0.x,gz0.x);
223:   vec3 g100 = vec3(gx0.y,gy0.y,gz0.y);
224:   vec3 g010 = vec3(gx0.z,gy0.z,gz0.z);
225:   vec3 g110 = vec3(gx0.w,gy0.w,gz0.w);
226:   vec3 g001 = vec3(gx1.x,gy1.x,gz1.x);
227:   vec3 g101 = vec3(gx1.y,gy1.y,gz1.y);
228:   vec3 g011 = vec3(gx1.z,gy1.z,gz1.z);
229:   vec3 g111 = vec3(gx1.w,gy1.w,gz1.w);
230: 
231:   vec4 norm0 = taylorInvSqrt(vec4(dot(g000, g000), dot(g010, g010), dot(g100, g100), dot(g110, g110)));
232:   g000 *= norm0.x;
233:   g010 *= norm0.y;
234:   g100 *= norm0.z;
235:   g110 *= norm0.w;
236:   vec4 norm1 = taylorInvSqrt(vec4(dot(g001, g001), dot(g011, g011), dot(g101, g101), dot(g111, g111)));
237:   g001 *= norm1.x;
238:   g011 *= norm1.y;
239:   g101 *= norm1.z;
240:   g111 *= norm1.w;
241: 
242:   float n000 = dot(g000, Pf0);
243:   float n100 = dot(g100, vec3(Pf1.x, Pf0.yz));
244:   float n010 = dot(g010, vec3(Pf0.x, Pf1.y, Pf0.z));
245:   float n110 = dot(g110, vec3(Pf1.xy, Pf0.z));
246:   float n001 = dot(g001, vec3(Pf0.xy, Pf1.z));
247:   float n101 = dot(g101, vec3(Pf1.x, Pf0.y, Pf1.z));
248:   float n011 = dot(g011, vec3(Pf0.x, Pf1.yz));
249:   float n111 = dot(g111, Pf1);
250: 
251:   vec3 fade_xyz = fade(Pf0);
252:   vec4 n_z = mix(vec4(n000, n100, n010, n110), vec4(n001, n101, n011, n111), fade_xyz.z);
253:   vec2 n_yz = mix(n_z.xy, n_z.zw, fade_xyz.y);
254:   float n_xyz = mix(n_yz.x, n_yz.y, fade_xyz.x);
255:   return 2.2 * n_xyz;
256: }
257: 
258: 
259: float random(vec2 p) {
260:     return fract(sin(dot(p, vec2(12.9898,78.233))) * 43758.5453);
261: }
262: 
263: float fbm(vec3 x) {
264:     float value = 0.0;
265:     float amplitude = 0.5;
266:     float frequency = 1.0;
267:     for (int i = 0; i < 4; i++) {
268:         value += amplitude * snoise(x * frequency);
269:         frequency *= 2.0;
270:         amplitude *= 0.5;
271:     }
272:     return value;
273: }
274: 
275: void main() {
276:     // MOUSE DISTORTION
277:     vec2 finalUv = vFlowUv;
278:     
279:     if (u_mouse_distortion_strength > 0.0) {
280:         vec4 mouseColor = texture2D(u_mouse_texture, vUv);
281:         float mouseValue = mouseColor.r;
282:         
283:         if (mouseValue > 0.001) {
284:             float distortionAmount = mouseValue * u_mouse_distortion_strength;
285:             vec2 mouseDisp = vec2(distortionAmount, distortionAmount);
286:             finalUv -= mouseDisp;
287:         }
288:     }
289:     
290:     vec3 baseColor;
291: 
292:     if (u_enable_procedural_texture > 0.5) {
293:         // Calculate flow field distance for ease effect
294:         vec2 ppp = -1.0 + 2.0 * finalUv;
295:         ppp += 0.1 * cos((1.5 * u_flow_scale) * ppp.yx + 1.1 * u_time + vec2(0.1, 1.1));
296:         ppp += 0.1 * cos((2.3 * u_flow_scale) * ppp.yx + 1.3 * u_time + vec2(3.2, 3.4));
297:         ppp += 0.1 * cos((2.2 * u_flow_scale) * ppp.yx + 1.7 * u_time + vec2(1.8, 5.2));
298:         ppp += u_flow_distortion_a * cos((u_flow_distortion_b * u_flow_scale) * ppp.yx + 1.4 * u_time + vec2(6.3, 3.9));
299:         float r = length(ppp); // Flow distance
300:         
301:         // Ease blending: 0 = topographic (flow), 1 = image (UV)
302:         float vx = (finalUv.x * u_texture_ease) + (r * (1.0 - u_texture_ease));
303:         float vy = (finalUv.y * u_texture_ease) + (0.0 * (1.0 - u_texture_ease));
304:         vec2 texUv = vec2(vx, vy);
305: 
306:         // PARALLAX SCROLLING
307:         // We manually apply a smaller offset here to make the texture lag behind
308:         float parallaxFactor = 0.25; // 25% speed of the color mixing
309:         texUv.y -= (u_y_offset * u_y_offset_color_multiplier / u_plane_height) * parallaxFactor;
310: 
311:         texUv *= 1.5; // Tiling scale
312: 
313:         vec4 texSample = texture2D(u_procedural_texture, texUv);
314:         baseColor = texSample.rgb;
315:     } else {
316:         baseColor = v_color;
317:     }
318: 
319:     vec3 color = baseColor;
320: 
321:     // Post-processing
322:     color += pow(v_displacement_amount, 1.0) * u_highlights;
323:     color -= pow(1.0 - v_displacement_amount, 2.0) * u_shadows;
324:     color = saturation(color, 1.0 + u_saturation);
325:     color = color * u_brightness;
326: 
327:     // Grain
328:     vec2 noiseCoords = gl_FragCoord.xy / u_grain_scale;
329:     float grain = (u_grain_speed != 0.0) ? fbm(vec3(noiseCoords, u_time * u_grain_speed)) : fbm(vec3(noiseCoords, 0.0));
330: 
331:     grain = grain * 0.5 + 0.5;
332:     grain -= 0.5;
333:     grain = (grain > u_grain_sparsity) ? grain : 0.0;
334:     grain *= u_grain_intensity;
335: 
336:     color += vec3(grain);
337: 
338:     gl_FragColor = vec4(color, 1.0);
339: }

59: // 1. REPLACEMENT PERMUTE: 
60: // Uses a hash function (fract/sin) instead of a modular lookup table.
61: vec4 permute(vec4 x) {
62:     return floor(fract(sin(x) * 43758.5453123) * 289.0);
63: }
64: 
65: // Taylor Inverse Sqrt
66: vec4 taylorInvSqrt(vec4 r) {
67:   return 1.79284291400159 - 0.85373472095314 * r;
68: }
69: 
70: // Fade function
71: vec3 fade(vec3 t) {
72:   return t*t*t*(t*(t*6.0-15.0)+10.0);
73: }

75: // 3D Simplex Noise
76: float snoise(vec3 v) {
77:   const vec2  C = vec2(1.0/6.0, 1.0/3.0) ;
78:   const vec4  D = vec4(0.0, 0.5, 1.0, 2.0);
79: 
80:   // First corner
81:   vec3 i  = floor(v + dot(v, C.yyy) );
82:   vec3 x0 =   v - i + dot(i, C.xxx) ;
83: 
84:   // Other corners
85:   vec3 g = step(x0.yzx, x0.xyz);
86:   vec3 l = 1.0 - g;
87:   vec3 i1 = min( g.xyz, l.zxy );
88:   vec3 i2 = max( g.xyz, l.zxy );
89: 
90:   vec3 x1 = x0 - i1 + C.xxx;
91:   vec3 x2 = x0 - i2 + C.yyy;
92:   vec3 x3 = x0 - D.yyy;
93: 
94:   // Permutations
95:   vec4 p = permute( permute( permute(
96:             i.z + vec4(0.0, i1.z, i2.z, 1.0 ))
97:           + i.y + vec4(0.0, i1.y, i2.y, 1.0 ))
98:           + i.x + vec4(0.0, i1.x, i2.x, 1.0 ));
99: 
100:   // Gradients
101:   float n_ = 0.142857142857; // 1.0/7.0
102:   vec3  ns = n_ * D.wyz - D.xzx;
103: 
104:   vec4 j = p - 49.0 * floor(p * ns.z * ns.z);
105: 
106:   vec4 x_ = floor(j * ns.z);
107:   vec4 y_ = floor(j - 7.0 * x_ );
108: 
109:   vec4 x = x_ *ns.x + ns.yyyy;
110:   vec4 y = y_ *ns.x + ns.yyyy;
111:   vec4 h = 1.0 - abs(x) - abs(y);
112: 
113:   vec4 b0 = vec4( x.xy, y.xy );
114:   vec4 b1 = vec4( x.zw, y.zw );
115: 
116:   vec4 s0 = floor(b0)*2.0 + 1.0;
117:   vec4 s1 = floor(b1)*2.0 + 1.0;
118:   vec4 sh = -step(h, vec4(0.0));
119: 
120:   vec4 a0 = b0.xzyw + s0.xzyw*sh.xxyy ;
121:   vec4 a1 = b1.xzyw + s1.xzyw*sh.zzww ;
122: 
123:   vec3 p0 = vec3(a0.xy,h.x);
124:   vec3 p1 = vec3(a0.zw,h.y);
125:   vec3 p2 = vec3(a1.xy,h.z);
126:   vec3 p3 = vec3(a1.zw,h.w);
127: 
128:   // Normalise gradients
129:   vec4 norm = taylorInvSqrt(vec4(dot(p0,p0), dot(p1,p1), dot(p2, p2), dot(p3,p3)));
130:   p0 *= norm.x;
131:   p1 *= norm.y;
132:   p2 *= norm.z;
133:   p3 *= norm.w;
134: 
135:   // Mix final noise value
136:   vec4 m = max(0.6 - vec4(dot(x0,x0), dot(x1,x1), dot(x2,x2), dot(x3,x3)), 0.0);
137:   m = m * m;
138:   return 42.0 * dot( m*m, vec4( dot(p0,x0), dot(p1,x1),
139:                                 dot(p2,x2), dot(p3,x3) ) );
140: }
141: 
142: // Classic Perlin noise
143: float cnoise(vec3 P)
144: {
145:   vec3 Pi0 = floor(P); 
146:   vec3 Pi1 = Pi0 + vec3(1.0); 
147:   
148:   vec3 Pf0 = fract(P); 
149:   vec3 Pf1 = Pf0 - vec3(1.0); 
150:   vec4 ix = vec4(Pi0.x, Pi1.x, Pi0.x, Pi1.x);
151:   vec4 iy = vec4(Pi0.yy, Pi1.yy);
152:   vec4 iz0 = Pi0.zzzz;
153:   vec4 iz1 = Pi1.zzzz;
154: 
155:   vec4 ixy = permute(permute(ix) + iy);
156:   vec4 ixy0 = permute(ixy + iz0);
157:   vec4 ixy1 = permute(ixy + iz1);
158: 
159:   vec4 gx0 = ixy0 * (1.0 / 7.0);
160:   vec4 gy0 = fract(floor(gx0) * (1.0 / 7.0)) - 0.5;
161:   gx0 = fract(gx0);
162:   vec4 gz0 = vec4(0.5) - abs(gx0) - abs(gy0);
163:   vec4 sz0 = step(gz0, vec4(0.0));
164:   gx0 -= sz0 * (step(0.0, gx0) - 0.5);
165:   gy0 -= sz0 * (step(0.0, gy0) - 0.5);
166: 
167:   vec4 gx1 = ixy1 * (1.0 / 7.0);
168:   vec4 gy1 = fract(floor(gx1) * (1.0 / 7.0)) - 0.5;
169:   gx1 = fract(gx1);
170:   vec4 gz1 = vec4(0.5) - abs(gx1) - abs(gy1);
171:   vec4 sz1 = step(gz1, vec4(0.0));
172:   gx1 -= sz1 * (step(0.0, gx1) - 0.5);
173:   gy1 -= sz1 * (step(0.0, gy1) - 0.5);
174: 
175:   vec3 g000 = vec3(gx0.x,gy0.x,gz0.x);
176:   vec3 g100 = vec3(gx0.y,gy0.y,gz0.y);
177:   vec3 g010 = vec3(gx0.z,gy0.z,gz0.z);
178:   vec3 g110 = vec3(gx0.w,gy0.w,gz0.w);
179:   vec3 g001 = vec3(gx1.x,gy1.x,gz1.x);
180:   vec3 g101 = vec3(gx1.y,gy1.y,gz1.y);
181:   vec3 g011 = vec3(gx1.z,gy1.z,gz1.z);
182:   vec3 g111 = vec3(gx1.w,gy1.w,gz1.w);
183: 
184:   vec4 norm0 = taylorInvSqrt(vec4(dot(g000, g000), dot(g010, g010), dot(g100, g100), dot(g110, g110)));
185:   g000 *= norm0.x;
186:   g010 *= norm0.y;
187:   g100 *= norm0.z;
188:   g110 *= norm0.w;
189:   vec4 norm1 = taylorInvSqrt(vec4(dot(g001, g001), dot(g011, g011), dot(g101, g101), dot(g111, g111)));
190:   g001 *= norm1.x;
191:   g011 *= norm1.y;
192:   g101 *= norm1.z;
193:   g111 *= norm1.w;
194: 
195:   float n000 = dot(g000, Pf0);
196:   float n100 = dot(g100, vec3(Pf1.x, Pf0.yz));
197:   float n010 = dot(g010, vec3(Pf0.x, Pf1.y, Pf0.z));
198:   float n110 = dot(g110, vec3(Pf1.xy, Pf0.z));
199:   float n001 = dot(g001, vec3(Pf0.xy, Pf1.z));
200:   float n101 = dot(g101, vec3(Pf1.x, Pf0.y, Pf1.z));
201:   float n011 = dot(g011, vec3(Pf0.x, Pf1.yz));
202:   float n111 = dot(g111, Pf1);
203: 
204:   vec3 fade_xyz = fade(Pf0);
205:   vec4 n_z = mix(vec4(n000, n100, n010, n110), vec4(n001, n101, n011, n111), fade_xyz.z);
206:   vec2 n_yz = mix(n_z.xy, n_z.zw, fade_xyz.y);
207:   float n_xyz = mix(n_yz.x, n_yz.y, fade_xyz.x);
208:   return 2.2 * n_xyz;
209: }
210: 
211: vec3 saturation(vec3 rgb, float adjustment) {
212:     const vec3 W = vec3(0.2125, 0.7154, 0.0721);
213:     vec3 intensity = vec3(dot(rgb, W));
214:     return mix(intensity, rgb, adjustment);
215: }
216: 
217: float get_saturation(vec3 rgb)
218: {
219:     vec4 K = vec4(0.0, -1.0 / 3.0, 2.0 / 3.0, -1.0);
220:     vec4 p = mix(vec4(rgb.bg, K.wz), vec4(rgb.gb, K.xy), step(rgb.b, rgb.g));
221:     vec4 q = mix(vec4(p.xyw, rgb.r), vec4(rgb.r, p.yzx), step(p.x, rgb.r));
222: 
223:     float d = q.x - min(q.w, q.y);
224:     float e = 1.0e-10;
225:     return abs(6.0 * d + e);
226: }
227: 
228: // get saturation of a color in values between 0 and 1
229: float getSaturationMix(vec3 color) {
230:     float max = max(color.r, max(color.g, color.b));
231:     float min = min(color.r, min(color.g, color.b));
232:     return (max - min) / max;
233: }
234:     
235: vec3 rgb2hsv(vec3 c)
236: {
237:     vec4 K = vec4(0.0, -1.0 / 3.0, 2.0 / 3.0, -1.0);
238:     vec4 p = mix(vec4(c.bg, K.wz), vec4(c.gb, K.xy), step(c.b, c.g));
239:     vec4 q = mix(vec4(p.xyw, c.r), vec4(c.r, p.yzx), step(p.x, c.r));
240: 
241:     float d = q.x - min(q.w, q.y);
242:     float e = 1.0e-10;
243:     return vec3(abs(q.z + (q.w - q.y) / (6.0 * d + e)), d / (q.x + e), q.x);
244: }
245: 
246: vec3 hsv2rgb(vec3 c)
247: {
248:     vec4 K = vec4(1.0, 2.0 / 3.0, 1.0 / 3.0, 3.0);
249:     vec3 p = abs(fract(c.xxx + K.xyz) * 6.0 - K.www);
250:     return c.z * mix(K.xxx, clamp(p - K.xxx, 0.0, 1.0), c.y);
251: }
252: 
253: // Color related helper functions
254: vec3 blendColors(vec3 colorA, vec3 colorB, float weight) {
255:     return mix(colorA, colorB, weight);
256: }

258: precision highp float;
259: 
260: attribute vec3 position;
261: attribute vec3 normal;
262: attribute vec2 uv;
263: 
264: uniform mat4 modelViewMatrix;
265: uniform mat4 projectionMatrix;
266: 
267: // Uniforms injected by THREE previously:
268: // NONE that we don't define manually here.
269: 
270: void main() {
271:     vUv = uv;
272: 
273:     // SCROLLING LOGIC
274:     // Separate multipliers for wave, color, and flow offsets
275:     float waveOffset = -u_y_offset * u_y_offset_wave_multiplier;
276:     float colorOffset = -u_y_offset * u_y_offset_color_multiplier;
277:     float flowOffset = -u_y_offset * u_y_offset_flow_multiplier;
278: 
279:     // 1. DISPLACEMENT (WAVES)
280:     // We add waveOffset to Y to scroll the wave pattern
281:     v_displacement_amount = cnoise( vec3(
282:         u_wave_frequency_x * position.x + u_time,
283:         u_wave_frequency_y * (position.y + waveOffset) + u_time,
284:         u_time
285:     ));
286: 
287:     // 2. FLOW FIELD
288:     // Apply flow offset to scroll the flow field mask
289:     vec2 baseUv = vUv;
290:     baseUv.y += flowOffset / u_plane_height; // Scale to match wave speed
291:     vec2 flowUv = baseUv;
292: 
293:     if (u_flow_enabled > 0.5) {
294:         if (u_flow_ease > 0.0 || u_flow_distortion_a > 0.0) {
295:             vec2 ppp = -1.0 + 2.0 * baseUv;
296:             ppp += 0.1 * cos((1.5 * u_flow_scale) * ppp.yx + 1.1 * u_time + vec2(0.1, 1.1));
297:             ppp += 0.1 * cos((2.3 * u_flow_scale) * ppp.yx + 1.3 * u_time + vec2(3.2, 3.4));
298:             ppp += 0.1 * cos((2.2 * u_flow_scale) * ppp.yx + 1.7 * u_time + vec2(1.8, 5.2));
299:             ppp += u_flow_distortion_a * cos((u_flow_distortion_b * u_flow_scale) * ppp.yx + 1.4 * u_time + vec2(6.3, 3.9));
300: 
301:             float r = length(ppp);
302:             flowUv = mix(baseUv, vec2(baseUv.x * (1.0 - u_flow_ease) + r * u_flow_ease, baseUv.y), u_flow_ease);
303:         }
304:     }
305: 
306:     // Pass the standard flow UV to fragment shader (for mouse/texture)
307:     vFlowUv = flowUv;
308: 
309:     // 3. COLOR MIXING
310:     // We take the computed flow UVs and apply the color offset
311:     // Scale by plane height to match wave offset speed (world space vs UV space)
312:     vec3 color = u_colors[0].color;
313:     // ...
314:     vec2 adjustedUv = flowUv;
315:     adjustedUv.y += colorOffset / u_plane_height; // Scroll the color mixing pattern
316: 
317:     vec2 noise_cord = adjustedUv * u_color_pressure;
318:     const float minNoise = .0;
319:     const float maxNoise = .9;
320: 
321:     for (int i = 1; i < 6; i++) {
322:         if(i >= u_colors_count) break;
323:         if(u_colors[i].is_active > 0.5){
324:             float noiseFlow = (1. + float(i)) / 30.;
325:             float noiseSpeed = (1. + float(i)) * 0.11;
326:             float noiseSeed = 13. + float(i) * 7.;
327: 
328:             float noise = snoise(
329:                 vec3(
330:                     noise_cord.x * u_color_pressure.x + u_time * noiseFlow * 2.,
331:                     noise_cord.y * u_color_pressure.y,
332:                     u_time * noiseSpeed
333:                 ) + noiseSeed
334:             ) - (.1 * float(i)) + (.5 * u_color_blending);
335: 
336:             noise = clamp(minNoise, maxNoise + float(i) * 0.02, noise);
337:             color = mix(color, u_colors[i].color, smoothstep(0.0, u_color_blending, noise));
338:         }
339:     }
340: 
341:     v_color = color;
342: 
343:     // 4. VERTEX POSITION
344:     vec3 newPosition = position + normal * v_displacement_amount * u_wave_amplitude;
345:     gl_Position = projectionMatrix * modelViewMatrix * vec4(newPosition, 1.0);
346:     v_new_position = gl_Position;
347: }

67:     vec4 K = vec4(0.0, -1.0 / 3.0, 2.0 / 3.0, -1.0);
68:     vec4 p = mix(vec4(rgb.bg, K.wz), vec4(rgb.gb, K.xy), step(rgb.b, rgb.g));
69:     vec4 q = mix(vec4(p.xyw, rgb.r), vec4(rgb.r, p.yzx), step(p.x, rgb.r));
70: 
71:     float d = q.x - min(q.w, q.y);
72:     float e = 1.0e-10;
73:     return abs(6.0 * d + e);
74: }
75: 
76: // get saturation of a color in values between 0 and 1
77: float getSaturationMix(vec3 color) {
78:     float max = max(color.r, max(color.g, color.b));
79:     float min = min(color.r, min(color.g, color.b));
80:     return (max - min) / max;
81: }
82:     
83: vec3 rgb2hsv(vec3 c)
84: {
85:     vec4 K = vec4(0.0, -1.0 / 3.0, 2.0 / 3.0, -1.0);
86:     vec4 p = mix(vec4(c.bg, K.wz), vec4(c.gb, K.xy), step(c.b, c.g));
87:     vec4 q = mix(vec4(p.xyw, c.r), vec4(c.r, p.yzx), step(p.x, c.r));
88: 
89:     float d = q.x - min(q.w, q.y);
90:     float e = 1.0e-10;
91:     return vec3(abs(q.z + (q.w - q.y) / (6.0 * d + e)), d / (q.x + e), q.x);
92: }
93: 
94: vec3 hsv2rgb(vec3 c)
95: {
96:     vec4 K = vec4(1.0, 2.0 / 3.0, 1.0 / 3.0, 3.0);
97:     vec3 p = abs(fract(c.xxx + K.xyz) * 6.0 - K.www);
98:     return c.z * mix(K.xxx, clamp(p - K.xxx, 0.0, 1.0), c.y);
99: }
100: 
101: // Color related helper functions
102: vec3 blendColors(vec3 colorA, vec3 colorB, float weight) {
103:     return mix(colorA, colorB, weight);
104: }
105: 
106: // 1. REPLACEMENT PERMUTE: 
107: // Uses a hash function (fract/sin) instead of a modular lookup table.
108: vec4 permute(vec4 x) {
109:     return floor(fract(sin(x) * 43758.5453123) * 289.0);
110: }
111: 
112: // Taylor Inverse Sqrt
113: vec4 taylorInvSqrt(vec4 r) {
114:   return 1.79284291400159 - 0.85373472095314 * r;
115: }
116: 
117: // Fade function
118: vec3 fade(vec3 t) {
119:   return t*t*t*(t*(t*6.0-15.0)+10.0);
120: }
121: 
122: // 3D Simplex Noise
123: float snoise(vec3 v) {
124:   const vec2  C = vec2(1.0/6.0, 1.0/3.0) ;
125:   const vec4  D = vec4(0.0, 0.5, 1.0, 2.0);
126: 
127:   // First corner
128:   vec3 i  = floor(v + dot(v, C.yyy) );
129:   vec3 x0 =   v - i + dot(i, C.xxx) ;
130: 
131:   // Other corners
132:   vec3 g = step(x0.yzx, x0.xyz);
133:   vec3 l = 1.0 - g;
134:   vec3 i1 = min( g.xyz, l.zxy );
135:   vec3 i2 = max( g.xyz, l.zxy );
136: 
137:   vec3 x1 = x0 - i1 + C.xxx;
138:   vec3 x2 = x0 - i2 + C.yyy;
139:   vec3 x3 = x0 - D.yyy;
140: 
141:   // Permutations
142:   vec4 p = permute( permute( permute(
143:             i.z + vec4(0.0, i1.z, i2.z, 1.0 ))
144:           + i.y + vec4(0.0, i1.y, i2.y, 1.0 ))
145:           + i.x + vec4(0.0, i1.x, i2.x, 1.0 ));
146: 
147:   // Gradients
148:   float n_ = 0.142857142857; // 1.0/7.0
149:   vec3  ns = n_ * D.wyz - D.xzx;
150: 
151:   vec4 j = p - 49.0 * floor(p * ns.z * ns.z);
152: 
153:   vec4 x_ = floor(j * ns.z);
154:   vec4 y_ = floor(j - 7.0 * x_ );
155: 
156:   vec4 x = x_ *ns.x + ns.yyyy;
157:   vec4 y = y_ *ns.x + ns.yyyy;
158:   vec4 h = 1.0 - abs(x) - abs(y);
159: 
160:   vec4 b0 = vec4( x.xy, y.xy );
161:   vec4 b1 = vec4( x.zw, y.zw );
162: 
163:   vec4 s0 = floor(b0)*2.0 + 1.0;
164:   vec4 s1 = floor(b1)*2.0 + 1.0;
165:   vec4 sh = -step(h, vec4(0.0));
166: 
167:   vec4 a0 = b0.xzyw + s0.xzyw*sh.xxyy ;
168:   vec4 a1 = b1.xzyw + s1.xzyw*sh.zzww ;
169: 
170:   vec3 p0 = vec3(a0.xy,h.x);
171:   vec3 p1 = vec3(a0.zw,h.y);
172:   vec3 p2 = vec3(a1.xy,h.z);
173:   vec3 p3 = vec3(a1.zw,h.w);
174: 
175:   // Normalise gradients
176:   vec4 norm = taylorInvSqrt(vec4(dot(p0,p0), dot(p1,p1), dot(p2, p2), dot(p3,p3)));
177:   p0 *= norm.x;
178:   p1 *= norm.y;
179:   p2 *= norm.z;
180:   p3 *= norm.w;
181: 
182:   // Mix final noise value
183:   vec4 m = max(0.6 - vec4(dot(x0,x0), dot(x1,x1), dot(x2,x2), dot(x3,x3)), 0.0);
184:   m = m * m;
185:   return 42.0 * dot( m*m, vec4( dot(p0,x0), dot(p1,x1),
186:                                 dot(p2,x2), dot(p3,x3) ) );
187: }
188: 
189: // Classic Perlin noise
190: float cnoise(vec3 P)
191: {
192:   vec3 Pi0 = floor(P); 
193:   vec3 Pi1 = Pi0 + vec3(1.0); 
194:   
195:   vec3 Pf0 = fract(P); 
196:   vec3 Pf1 = Pf0 - vec3(1.0); 
197:   vec4 ix = vec4(Pi0.x, Pi1.x, Pi0.x, Pi1.x);
198:   vec4 iy = vec4(Pi0.yy, Pi1.yy);
199:   vec4 iz0 = Pi0.zzzz;
200:   vec4 iz1 = Pi1.zzzz;
201: 
202:   vec4 ixy = permute(permute(ix) + iy);
203:   vec4 ixy0 = permute(ixy + iz0);
204:   vec4 ixy1 = permute(ixy + iz1);
205: 
206:   vec4 gx0 = ixy0 * (1.0 / 7.0);
207:   vec4 gy0 = fract(floor(gx0) * (1.0 / 7.0)) - 0.5;
208:   gx0 = fract(gx0);
209:   vec4 gz0 = vec4(0.5) - abs(gx0) - abs(gy0);
210:   vec4 sz0 = step(gz0, vec4(0.0));
211:   gx0 -= sz0 * (step(0.0, gx0) - 0.5);
212:   gy0 -= sz0 * (step(0.0, gy0) - 0.5);
213: 
214:   vec4 gx1 = ixy1 * (1.0 / 7.0);
215:   vec4 gy1 = fract(floor(gx1) * (1.0 / 7.0)) - 0.5;
216:   gx1 = fract(gx1);
217:   vec4 gz1 = vec4(0.5) - abs(gx1) - abs(gy1);
218:   vec4 sz1 = step(gz1, vec4(0.0));
219:   gx1 -= sz1 * (step(0.0, gx1) - 0.5);
220:   gy1 -= sz1 * (step(0.0, gy1) - 0.5);
221: 
222:   vec3 g000 = vec3(gx0.x,gy0.x,gz0.x);
223:   vec3 g100 = vec3(gx0.y,gy0.y,gz0.y);
224:   vec3 g010 = vec3(gx0.z,gy0.z,gz0.z);
225:   vec3 g110 = vec3(gx0.w,gy0.w,gz0.w);
226:   vec3 g001 = vec3(gx1.x,gy1.x,gz1.x);
227:   vec3 g101 = vec3(gx1.y,gy1.y,gz1.y);
228:   vec3 g011 = vec3(gx1.z,gy1.z,gz1.z);
229:   vec3 g111 = vec3(gx1.w,gy1.w,gz1.w);
230: 
231:   vec4 norm0 = taylorInvSqrt(vec4(dot(g000, g000), dot(g010, g010), dot(g100, g100), dot(g110, g110)));
232:   g000 *= norm0.x;
233:   g010 *= norm0.y;
234:   g100 *= norm0.z;
235:   g110 *= norm0.w;
236:   vec4 norm1 = taylorInvSqrt(vec4(dot(g001, g001), dot(g011, g011), dot(g101, g101), dot(g111, g111)));
237:   g001 *= norm1.x;
238:   g011 *= norm1.y;
239:   g101 *= norm1.z;
240:   g111 *= norm1.w;
241: 
242:   float n000 = dot(g000, Pf0);
243:   float n100 = dot(g100, vec3(Pf1.x, Pf0.yz));
244:   float n010 = dot(g010, vec3(Pf0.x, Pf1.y, Pf0.z));
245:   float n110 = dot(g110, vec3(Pf1.xy, Pf0.z));
246:   float n001 = dot(g001, vec3(Pf0.xy, Pf1.z));
247:   float n101 = dot(g101, vec3(Pf1.x, Pf0.y, Pf1.z));
248:   float n011 = dot(g011, vec3(Pf0.x, Pf1.yz));
249:   float n111 = dot(g111, Pf1);
250: 
251:   vec3 fade_xyz = fade(Pf0);
252:   vec4 n_z = mix(vec4(n000, n100, n010, n110), vec4(n001, n101, n011, n111), fade_xyz.z);
253:   vec2 n_yz = mix(n_z.xy, n_z.zw, fade_xyz.y);
254:   float n_xyz = mix(n_yz.x, n_yz.y, fade_xyz.x);
255:   return 2.2 * n_xyz;
256: }
257: 
258: 
259: float random(vec2 p) {
260:     return fract(sin(dot(p, vec2(12.9898,78.233))) * 43758.5453);
261: }
262: 
263: float fbm(vec3 x) {
264:     float value = 0.0;
265:     float amplitude = 0.5;
266:     float frequency = 1.0;
267:     for (int i = 0; i < 4; i++) {
268:         value += amplitude * snoise(x * frequency);
269:         frequency *= 2.0;
270:         amplitude *= 0.5;
271:     }
272:     return value;
273: }
274: 
275: void main() {
276:     // MOUSE DISTORTION
277:     vec2 finalUv = vFlowUv;
278:     
279:     if (u_mouse_distortion_strength > 0.0) {
280:         vec4 mouseColor = texture2D(u_mouse_texture, vUv);
281:         float mouseValue = mouseColor.r;
282:         
283:         if (mouseValue > 0.001) {
284:             float distortionAmount = mouseValue * u_mouse_distortion_strength;
285:             vec2 mouseDisp = vec2(distortionAmount, distortionAmount);
286:             finalUv -= mouseDisp;
287:         }
288:     }
289:     
290:     vec3 baseColor;
291: 
292:     if (u_enable_procedural_texture > 0.5) {
293:         // Calculate flow field distance for ease effect
294:         vec2 ppp = -1.0 + 2.0 * finalUv;
295:         ppp += 0.1 * cos((1.5 * u_flow_scale) * ppp.yx + 1.1 * u_time + vec2(0.1, 1.1));
296:         ppp += 0.1 * cos((2.3 * u_flow_scale) * ppp.yx + 1.3 * u_time + vec2(3.2, 3.4));
297:         ppp += 0.1 * cos((2.2 * u_flow_scale) * ppp.yx + 1.7 * u_time + vec2(1.8, 5.2));
298:         ppp += u_flow_distortion_a * cos((u_flow_distortion_b * u_flow_scale) * ppp.yx + 1.4 * u_time + vec2(6.3, 3.9));
299:         float r = length(ppp); // Flow distance
300:         
301:         // Ease blending: 0 = topographic (flow), 1 = image (UV)
302:         float vx = (finalUv.x * u_texture_ease) + (r * (1.0 - u_texture_ease));
303:         float vy = (finalUv.y * u_texture_ease) + (0.0 * (1.0 - u_texture_ease));
304:         vec2 texUv = vec2(vx, vy);
305: 
306:         // PARALLAX SCROLLING
307:         // We manually apply a smaller offset here to make the texture lag behind
308:         float parallaxFactor = 0.25; // 25% speed of the color mixing
309:         texUv.y -= (u_y_offset * u_y_offset_color_multiplier / u_plane_height) * parallaxFactor;
310: 
311:         texUv *= 1.5; // Tiling scale
312: 
313:         vec4 texSample = texture2D(u_procedural_texture, texUv);
314:         baseColor = texSample.rgb;
315:     } else {
316:         baseColor = v_color;
317:     }
318: 
319:     vec3 color = baseColor;
320: 
321:     // Post-processing
322:     color += pow(v_displacement_amount, 1.0) * u_highlights;
323:     color -= pow(1.0 - v_displacement_amount, 2.0) * u_shadows;
324:     color = saturation(color, 1.0 + u_saturation);
325:     color = color * u_brightness;
326: 
327:     // Grain
328:     vec2 noiseCoords = gl_FragCoord.xy / u_grain_scale;
329:     float grain = (u_grain_speed != 0.0) ? fbm(vec3(noiseCoords, u_time * u_grain_speed)) : fbm(vec3(noiseCoords, 0.0));
330: 
331:     grain = grain * 0.5 + 0.5;
332:     grain -= 0.5;
333:     grain = (grain > u_grain_sparsity) ? grain : 0.0;
334:     grain *= u_grain_intensity;
335: 
336:     color += vec3(grain);
337: 
338:     gl_FragColor = vec4(color, 1.0);
339: }

98:           + i.x + vec4(0.0, i1.x, i2.x, 1.0 ));

114:   vec4 b1 = vec4( x.zw, y.zw );

198:   float n110 = dot(g110, vec3(Pf1.xy, Pf0.z));
199:   float n001 = dot(g001, vec3(Pf0.xy, Pf1.z));
200:   float n101 = dot(g101, vec3(Pf1.x, Pf0.y, Pf1.z));
201:   float n011 = dot(g011, vec3(Pf0.x, Pf1.yz));
202:   float n111 = dot(g111, Pf1);
203: 
204:   vec3 fade_xyz = fade(Pf0);
205:   vec4 n_z = mix(vec4(n000, n100, n010, n110), vec4(n001, n101, n011, n111), fade_xyz.z);
206:   vec2 n_yz = mix(n_z.xy, n_z.zw, fade_xyz.y);
207:   float n_xyz = mix(n_yz.x, n_yz.y, fade_xyz.x);
208:   return 2.2 * n_xyz;
209: }
210: 
211: vec3 saturation(vec3 rgb, float adjustment) {
212:     const vec3 W = vec3(0.2125, 0.7154, 0.0721);
213:     vec3 intensity = vec3(dot(rgb, W));
214:     return mix(intensity, rgb, adjustment);
215: }
216: 
217: float get_saturation(vec3 rgb)
218: {
219:     vec4 K = vec4(0.0, -1.0 / 3.0, 2.0 / 3.0, -1.0);
220:     vec4 p = mix(vec4(rgb.bg, K.wz), vec4(rgb.gb, K.xy), step(rgb.b, rgb.g));
221:     vec4 q = mix(vec4(p.xyw, rgb.r), vec4(rgb.r, p.yzx), step(p.x, rgb.r));
222: 
223:     float d = q.x - min(q.w, q.y);
224:     float e = 1.0e-10;
225:     return abs(6.0 * d + e);
226: }
227: 
228: // get saturation of a color in values between 0 and 1
229: float getSaturationMix(vec3 color) {
230:     float max = max(color.r, max(color.g, color.b));
231:     float min = min(color.r, min(color.g, color.b));
232:     return (max - min) / max;
233: }
234:     
235: vec3 rgb2hsv(vec3 c)
236: {
237:     vec4 K = vec4(0.0, -1.0 / 3.0, 2.0 / 3.0, -1.0);
238:     vec4 p = mix(vec4(c.bg, K.wz), vec4(c.gb, K.xy), step(c.b, c.g));
239:     vec4 q = mix(vec4(p.xyw, c.r), vec4(c.r, p.yzx), step(p.x, c.r));
240: 
241:     float d = q.x - min(q.w, q.y);
242:     float e = 1.0e-10;
243:     return vec3(abs(q.z + (q.w - q.y) / (6.0 * d + e)), d / (q.x + e), q.x);
244: }
245: 
246: vec3 hsv2rgb(vec3 c)
247: {
248:     vec4 K = vec4(1.0, 2.0 / 3.0, 1.0 / 3.0, 3.0);
249:     vec3 p = abs(fract(c.xxx + K.xyz) * 6.0 - K.www);
250:     return c.z * mix(K.xxx, clamp(p - K.xxx, 0.0, 1.0), c.y);
251: }
252: 
253: // Color related helper functions
254: vec3 blendColors(vec3 colorA, vec3 colorB, float weight) {
255:     return mix(colorA, colorB, weight);
256: }

265: uniform mat4 projectionMatrix;

267: // Uniforms injected by THREE previously:
268: // NONE that we don't define manually here.
269: 
270: void main() {
271:     vUv = uv;
272: 
273:     // SCROLLING LOGIC
274:     // Separate multipliers for wave, color, and flow offsets
275:     float waveOffset = -u_y_offset * u_y_offset_wave_multiplier;
276:     float colorOffset = -u_y_offset * u_y_offset_color_multiplier;
277:     float flowOffset = -u_y_offset * u_y_offset_flow_multiplier;
278: 
279:     // 1. DISPLACEMENT (WAVES)
280:     // We add waveOffset to Y to scroll the wave pattern
281:     v_displacement_amount = cnoise( vec3(
282:         u_wave_frequency_x * position.x + u_time,
283:         u_wave_frequency_y * (position.y + waveOffset) + u_time,
284:         u_time
285:     ));
286: 
287:     // 2. FLOW FIELD
288:     // Apply flow offset to scroll the flow field mask
289:     vec2 baseUv = vUv;
290:     baseUv.y += flowOffset / u_plane_height; // Scale to match wave speed
291:     vec2 flowUv = baseUv;
292: 
293:     if (u_flow_enabled > 0.5) {
294:         if (u_flow_ease > 0.0 || u_flow_distortion_a > 0.0) {
295:             vec2 ppp = -1.0 + 2.0 * baseUv;
296:             ppp += 0.1 * cos((1.5 * u_flow_scale) * ppp.yx + 1.1 * u_time + vec2(0.1, 1.1));
297:             ppp += 0.1 * cos((2.3 * u_flow_scale) * ppp.yx + 1.3 * u_time + vec2(3.2, 3.4));
298:             ppp += 0.1 * cos((2.2 * u_flow_scale) * ppp.yx + 1.7 * u_time + vec2(1.8, 5.2));
299:             ppp += u_flow_distortion_a * cos((u_flow_distortion_b * u_flow_scale) * ppp.yx + 1.4 * u_time + vec2(6.3, 3.9));
300: 
301:             float r = length(ppp);
302:             flowUv = mix(baseUv, vec2(baseUv.x * (1.0 - u_flow_ease) + r * u_flow_ease, baseUv.y), u_flow_ease);
303:         }
304:     }
305: 
306:     // Pass the standard flow UV to fragment shader (for mouse/texture)
307:     vFlowUv = flowUv;
308: 
309:     // 3. COLOR MIXING
310:     // We take the computed flow UVs and apply the color offset
311:     // Scale by plane height to match wave offset speed (world space vs UV space)
312:     vec3 color = u_colors[0].color;
313:     // ...
314:     vec2 adjustedUv = flowUv;
315:     adjustedUv.y += colorOffset / u_plane_height; // Scroll the color mixing pattern
316: 
317:     vec2 noise_cord = adjustedUv * u_color_pressure;
318:     const float minNoise = .0;
319:     const float maxNoise = .9;
320: 
321:     for (int i = 1; i < 6; i++) {
322:         if(i >= u_colors_count) break;
323:         if(u_colors[i].is_active > 0.5){
324:             float noiseFlow = (1. + float(i)) / 30.;
325:             float noiseSpeed = (1. + float(i)) * 0.11;
326:             float noiseSeed = 13. + float(i) * 7.;
327: 
328:             float noise = snoise(
329:                 vec3(
330:                     noise_cord.x * u_color_pressure.x + u_time * noiseFlow * 2.,
331:                     noise_cord.y * u_color_pressure.y,
332:                     u_time * noiseSpeed
333:                 ) + noiseSeed
334:             ) - (.1 * float(i)) + (.5 * u_color_blending);
335: 
336:             noise = clamp(minNoise, maxNoise + float(i) * 0.02, noise);
337:             color = mix(color, u_colors[i].color, smoothstep(0.0, u_color_blending, noise));
338:         }
339:     }
340: 
341:     v_color = color;
342: 
343:     // 4. VERTEX POSITION
344:     vec3 newPosition = position + normal * v_displacement_amount * u_wave_amplitude;
345:     gl_Position = projectionMatrix * modelViewMatrix * vec4(newPosition, 1.0);
346:     v_new_position = gl_Position;
347: }

106: // 1. REPLACEMENT PERMUTE: 
107: // Uses a hash function (fract/sin) instead of a modular lookup table.
108: vec4 permute(vec4 x) {
109:     return floor(fract(sin(x) * 43758.5453123) * 289.0);
110: }
111: 
112: // Taylor Inverse Sqrt
113: vec4 taylorInvSqrt(vec4 r) {
114:   return 1.79284291400159 - 0.85373472095314 * r;
115: }
116: 
117: // Fade function
118: vec3 fade(vec3 t) {
119:   return t*t*t*(t*(t*6.0-15.0)+10.0);
120: }
121: 
122: // 3D Simplex Noise
123: float snoise(vec3 v) {
124:   const vec2  C = vec2(1.0/6.0, 1.0/3.0) ;
125:   const vec4  D = vec4(0.0, 0.5, 1.0, 2.0);
126: 
127:   // First corner
128:   vec3 i  = floor(v + dot(v, C.yyy) );
129:   vec3 x0 =   v - i + dot(i, C.xxx) ;
130: 
131:   // Other corners
132:   vec3 g = step(x0.yzx, x0.xyz);
133:   vec3 l = 1.0 - g;
134:   vec3 i1 = min( g.xyz, l.zxy );
135:   vec3 i2 = max( g.xyz, l.zxy );
136: 
137:   vec3 x1 = x0 - i1 + C.xxx;
138:   vec3 x2 = x0 - i2 + C.yyy;
139:   vec3 x3 = x0 - D.yyy;
140: 
141:   // Permutations
142:   vec4 p = permute( permute( permute(
143:             i.z + vec4(0.0, i1.z, i2.z, 1.0 ))
144:           + i.y + vec4(0.0, i1.y, i2.y, 1.0 ))
145:           + i.x + vec4(0.0, i1.x, i2.x, 1.0 ));
146: 
147:   // Gradients
148:   float n_ = 0.142857142857; // 1.0/7.0
149:   vec3  ns = n_ * D.wyz - D.xzx;
150: 
151:   vec4 j = p - 49.0 * floor(p * ns.z * ns.z);
152: 
153:   vec4 x_ = floor(j * ns.z);
154:   vec4 y_ = floor(j - 7.0 * x_ );
155: 
156:   vec4 x = x_ *ns.x + ns.yyyy;
157:   vec4 y = y_ *ns.x + ns.yyyy;
158:   vec4 h = 1.0 - abs(x) - abs(y);
159: 
160:   vec4 b0 = vec4( x.xy, y.xy );
161:   vec4 b1 = vec4( x.zw, y.zw );
162: 
163:   vec4 s0 = floor(b0)*2.0 + 1.0;
164:   vec4 s1 = floor(b1)*2.0 + 1.0;
165:   vec4 sh = -step(h, vec4(0.0));
166: 
167:   vec4 a0 = b0.xzyw + s0.xzyw*sh.xxyy ;
168:   vec4 a1 = b1.xzyw + s1.xzyw*sh.zzww ;
169: 
170:   vec3 p0 = vec3(a0.xy,h.x);
171:   vec3 p1 = vec3(a0.zw,h.y);
172:   vec3 p2 = vec3(a1.xy,h.z);
173:   vec3 p3 = vec3(a1.zw,h.w);
174: 
175:   // Normalise gradients
176:   vec4 norm = taylorInvSqrt(vec4(dot(p0,p0), dot(p1,p1), dot(p2, p2), dot(p3,p3)));
177:   p0 *= norm.x;
178:   p1 *= norm.y;
179:   p2 *= norm.z;
180:   p3 *= norm.w;
181: 
182:   // Mix final noise value
183:   vec4 m = max(0.6 - vec4(dot(x0,x0), dot(x1,x1), dot(x2,x2), dot(x3,x3)), 0.0);
184:   m = m * m;
185:   return 42.0 * dot( m*m, vec4( dot(p0,x0), dot(p1,x1),
186:                                 dot(p2,x2), dot(p3,x3) ) );
187: }
188: 
189: // Classic Perlin noise
190: float cnoise(vec3 P)
191: {
192:   vec3 Pi0 = floor(P); 
193:   vec3 Pi1 = Pi0 + vec3(1.0); 
194:   
195:   vec3 Pf0 = fract(P); 
196:   vec3 Pf1 = Pf0 - vec3(1.0); 
197:   vec4 ix = vec4(Pi0.x, Pi1.x, Pi0.x, Pi1.x);
198:   vec4 iy = vec4(Pi0.yy, Pi1.yy);
199:   vec4 iz0 = Pi0.zzzz;
200:   vec4 iz1 = Pi1.zzzz;
201: 
202:   vec4 ixy = permute(permute(ix) + iy);
203:   vec4 ixy0 = permute(ixy + iz0);
204:   vec4 ixy1 = permute(ixy + iz1);
205: 
206:   vec4 gx0 = ixy0 * (1.0 / 7.0);
207:   vec4 gy0 = fract(floor(gx0) * (1.0 / 7.0)) - 0.5;
208:   gx0 = fract(gx0);
209:   vec4 gz0 = vec4(0.5) - abs(gx0) - abs(gy0);
210:   vec4 sz0 = step(gz0, vec4(0.0));
211:   gx0 -= sz0 * (step(0.0, gx0) - 0.5);
212:   gy0 -= sz0 * (step(0.0, gy0) - 0.5);
213: 
214:   vec4 gx1 = ixy1 * (1.0 / 7.0);
215:   vec4 gy1 = fract(floor(gx1) * (1.0 / 7.0)) - 0.5;
216:   gx1 = fract(gx1);
217:   vec4 gz1 = vec4(0.5) - abs(gx1) - abs(gy1);
218:   vec4 sz1 = step(gz1, vec4(0.0));
219:   gx1 -= sz1 * (step(0.0, gx1) - 0.5);
220:   gy1 -= sz1 * (step(0.0, gy1) - 0.5);
221: 
222:   vec3 g000 = vec3(gx0.x,gy0.x,gz0.x);
223:   vec3 g100 = vec3(gx0.y,gy0.y,gz0.y);
224:   vec3 g010 = vec3(gx0.z,gy0.z,gz0.z);
225:   vec3 g110 = vec3(gx0.w,gy0.w,gz0.w);
226:   vec3 g001 = vec3(gx1.x,gy1.x,gz1.x);
227:   vec3 g101 = vec3(gx1.y,gy1.y,gz1.y);
228:   vec3 g011 = vec3(gx1.z,gy1.z,gz1.z);
229:   vec3 g111 = vec3(gx1.w,gy1.w,gz1.w);
230: 
231:   vec4 norm0 = taylorInvSqrt(vec4(dot(g000, g000), dot(g010, g010), dot(g100, g100), dot(g110, g110)));
232:   g000 *= norm0.x;
233:   g010 *= norm0.y;
234:   g100 *= norm0.z;
235:   g110 *= norm0.w;
236:   vec4 norm1 = taylorInvSqrt(vec4(dot(g001, g001), dot(g011, g011), dot(g101, g101), dot(g111, g111)));
237:   g001 *= norm1.x;
238:   g011 *= norm1.y;
239:   g101 *= norm1.z;
240:   g111 *= norm1.w;
241: 
242:   float n000 = dot(g000, Pf0);
243:   float n100 = dot(g100, vec3(Pf1.x, Pf0.yz));
244:   float n010 = dot(g010, vec3(Pf0.x, Pf1.y, Pf0.z));
245:   float n110 = dot(g110, vec3(Pf1.xy, Pf0.z));
246:   float n001 = dot(g001, vec3(Pf0.xy, Pf1.z));
247:   float n101 = dot(g101, vec3(Pf1.x, Pf0.y, Pf1.z));
248:   float n011 = dot(g011, vec3(Pf0.x, Pf1.yz));
249:   float n111 = dot(g111, Pf1);
250: 
251:   vec3 fade_xyz = fade(Pf0);
252:   vec4 n_z = mix(vec4(n000, n100, n010, n110), vec4(n001, n101, n011, n111), fade_xyz.z);
253:   vec2 n_yz = mix(n_z.xy, n_z.zw, fade_xyz.y);
254:   float n_xyz = mix(n_yz.x, n_yz.y, fade_xyz.x);
255:   return 2.2 * n_xyz;
256: }
257: 
258: 
259: float random(vec2 p) {
260:     return fract(sin(dot(p, vec2(12.9898,78.233))) * 43758.5453);
261: }
262: 
263: float fbm(vec3 x) {
264:     float value = 0.0;
265:     float amplitude = 0.5;
266:     float frequency = 1.0;
267:     for (int i = 0; i < 4; i++) {
268:         value += amplitude * snoise(x * frequency);
269:         frequency *= 2.0;
270:         amplitude *= 0.5;
271:     }
272:     return value;
273: }
274: 
275: void main() {
276:     // MOUSE DISTORTION
277:     vec2 finalUv = vFlowUv;
278:     
279:     if (u_mouse_distortion_strength > 0.0) {
280:         vec4 mouseColor = texture2D(u_mouse_texture, vUv);
281:         float mouseValue = mouseColor.r;
282:         
283:         if (mouseValue > 0.001) {
284:             float distortionAmount = mouseValue * u_mouse_distortion_strength;
285:             vec2 mouseDisp = vec2(distortionAmount, distortionAmount);
286:             finalUv -= mouseDisp;
287:         }
288:     }
289:     
290:     vec3 baseColor;
291: 
292:     if (u_enable_procedural_texture > 0.5) {
293:         // Calculate flow field distance for ease effect
294:         vec2 ppp = -1.0 + 2.0 * finalUv;
295:         ppp += 0.1 * cos((1.5 * u_flow_scale) * ppp.yx + 1.1 * u_time + vec2(0.1, 1.1));
296:         ppp += 0.1 * cos((2.3 * u_flow_scale) * ppp.yx + 1.3 * u_time + vec2(3.2, 3.4));
297:         ppp += 0.1 * cos((2.2 * u_flow_scale) * ppp.yx + 1.7 * u_time + vec2(1.8, 5.2));
298:         ppp += u_flow_distortion_a * cos((u_flow_distortion_b * u_flow_scale) * ppp.yx + 1.4 * u_time + vec2(6.3, 3.9));
299:         float r = length(ppp); // Flow distance
300:         
301:         // Ease blending: 0 = topographic (flow), 1 = image (UV)
302:         float vx = (finalUv.x * u_texture_ease) + (r * (1.0 - u_texture_ease));
303:         float vy = (finalUv.y * u_texture_ease) + (0.0 * (1.0 - u_texture_ease));
304:         vec2 texUv = vec2(vx, vy);
305: 
306:         // PARALLAX SCROLLING
307:         // We manually apply a smaller offset here to make the texture lag behind
308:         float parallaxFactor = 0.25; // 25% speed of the color mixing
309:         texUv.y -= (u_y_offset * u_y_offset_color_multiplier / u_plane_height) * parallaxFactor;
310: 
311:         texUv *= 1.5; // Tiling scale
312: 
313:         vec4 texSample = texture2D(u_procedural_texture, texUv);
314:         baseColor = texSample.rgb;
315:     } else {
316:         baseColor = v_color;
317:     }
318: 
319:     vec3 color = baseColor;
320: 
321:     // Post-processing
322:     color += pow(v_displacement_amount, 1.0) * u_highlights;
323:     color -= pow(1.0 - v_displacement_amount, 2.0) * u_shadows;
324:     color = saturation(color, 1.0 + u_saturation);
325:     color = color * u_brightness;
326: 
327:     // Grain
328:     vec2 noiseCoords = gl_FragCoord.xy / u_grain_scale;
329:     float grain = (u_grain_speed != 0.0) ? fbm(vec3(noiseCoords, u_time * u_grain_speed)) : fbm(vec3(noiseCoords, 0.0));
330: 
331:     grain = grain * 0.5 + 0.5;
332:     grain -= 0.5;
333:     grain = (grain > u_grain_sparsity) ? grain : 0.0;
334:     grain *= u_grain_intensity;
335: 
336:     color += vec3(grain);
337: 
338:     gl_FragColor = vec4(color, 1.0);
339: }

59: // 1. REPLACEMENT PERMUTE: 
60: // Uses a hash function (fract/sin) instead of a modular lookup table.
61: vec4 permute(vec4 x) {
62:     return floor(fract(sin(x) * 43758.5453123) * 289.0);
63: }

65: // Taylor Inverse Sqrt
66: vec4 taylorInvSqrt(vec4 r) {
67:   return 1.79284291400159 - 0.85373472095314 * r;
68: }

75: // 3D Simplex Noise
76: float snoise(vec3 v) {
77:   const vec2  C = vec2(1.0/6.0, 1.0/3.0) ;
78:   const vec4  D = vec4(0.0, 0.5, 1.0, 2.0);
79: 
80:   // First corner
81:   vec3 i  = floor(v + dot(v, C.yyy) );
82:   vec3 x0 =   v - i + dot(i, C.xxx) ;
83: 
84:   // Other corners
85:   vec3 g = step(x0.yzx, x0.xyz);
86:   vec3 l = 1.0 - g;
87:   vec3 i1 = min( g.xyz, l.zxy );
88:   vec3 i2 = max( g.xyz, l.zxy );
89: 
90:   vec3 x1 = x0 - i1 + C.xxx;
91:   vec3 x2 = x0 - i2 + C.yyy;
92:   vec3 x3 = x0 - D.yyy;
93: 
94:   // Permutations
95:   vec4 p = permute( permute( permute(
96:             i.z + vec4(0.0, i1.z, i2.z, 1.0 ))
97:           + i.y + vec4(0.0, i1.y, i2.y, 1.0 ))
98:           + i.x + vec4(0.0, i1.x, i2.x, 1.0 ));
99: 
100:   // Gradients
101:   float n_ = 0.142857142857; // 1.0/7.0
102:   vec3  ns = n_ * D.wyz - D.xzx;
103: 
104:   vec4 j = p - 49.0 * floor(p * ns.z * ns.z);
105: 
106:   vec4 x_ = floor(j * ns.z);
107:   vec4 y_ = floor(j - 7.0 * x_ );
108: 
109:   vec4 x = x_ *ns.x + ns.yyyy;
110:   vec4 y = y_ *ns.x + ns.yyyy;
111:   vec4 h = 1.0 - abs(x) - abs(y);
112: 
113:   vec4 b0 = vec4( x.xy, y.xy );
114:   vec4 b1 = vec4( x.zw, y.zw );
115: 
116:   vec4 s0 = floor(b0)*2.0 + 1.0;
117:   vec4 s1 = floor(b1)*2.0 + 1.0;
118:   vec4 sh = -step(h, vec4(0.0));
119: 
120:   vec4 a0 = b0.xzyw + s0.xzyw*sh.xxyy ;
121:   vec4 a1 = b1.xzyw + s1.xzyw*sh.zzww ;
122: 
123:   vec3 p0 = vec3(a0.xy,h.x);
124:   vec3 p1 = vec3(a0.zw,h.y);
125:   vec3 p2 = vec3(a1.xy,h.z);
126:   vec3 p3 = vec3(a1.zw,h.w);
127: 
128:   // Normalise gradients
129:   vec4 norm = taylorInvSqrt(vec4(dot(p0,p0), dot(p1,p1), dot(p2, p2), dot(p3,p3)));
130:   p0 *= norm.x;
131:   p1 *= norm.y;
132:   p2 *= norm.z;
133:   p3 *= norm.w;
134: 
135:   // Mix final noise value
136:   vec4 m = max(0.6 - vec4(dot(x0,x0), dot(x1,x1), dot(x2,x2), dot(x3,x3)), 0.0);
137:   m = m * m;
138:   return 42.0 * dot( m*m, vec4( dot(p0,x0), dot(p1,x1),
139:                                 dot(p2,x2), dot(p3,x3) ) );
140: }
141: 
142: // Classic Perlin noise
143: float cnoise(vec3 P)
144: {
145:   vec3 Pi0 = floor(P); 
146:   vec3 Pi1 = Pi0 + vec3(1.0); 
147:   
148:   vec3 Pf0 = fract(P); 
149:   vec3 Pf1 = Pf0 - vec3(1.0); 
150:   vec4 ix = vec4(Pi0.x, Pi1.x, Pi0.x, Pi1.x);
151:   vec4 iy = vec4(Pi0.yy, Pi1.yy);
152:   vec4 iz0 = Pi0.zzzz;
153:   vec4 iz1 = Pi1.zzzz;
154: 
155:   vec4 ixy = permute(permute(ix) + iy);
156:   vec4 ixy0 = permute(ixy + iz0);
157:   vec4 ixy1 = permute(ixy + iz1);
158: 
159:   vec4 gx0 = ixy0 * (1.0 / 7.0);
160:   vec4 gy0 = fract(floor(gx0) * (1.0 / 7.0)) - 0.5;
161:   gx0 = fract(gx0);
162:   vec4 gz0 = vec4(0.5) - abs(gx0) - abs(gy0);
163:   vec4 sz0 = step(gz0, vec4(0.0));
164:   gx0 -= sz0 * (step(0.0, gx0) - 0.5);
165:   gy0 -= sz0 * (step(0.0, gy0) - 0.5);
166: 
167:   vec4 gx1 = ixy1 * (1.0 / 7.0);
168:   vec4 gy1 = fract(floor(gx1) * (1.0 / 7.0)) - 0.5;
169:   gx1 = fract(gx1);
170:   vec4 gz1 = vec4(0.5) - abs(gx1) - abs(gy1);
171:   vec4 sz1 = step(gz1, vec4(0.0));
172:   gx1 -= sz1 * (step(0.0, gx1) - 0.5);
173:   gy1 -= sz1 * (step(0.0, gy1) - 0.5);
174: 
175:   vec3 g000 = vec3(gx0.x,gy0.x,gz0.x);
176:   vec3 g100 = vec3(gx0.y,gy0.y,gz0.y);
177:   vec3 g010 = vec3(gx0.z,gy0.z,gz0.z);
178:   vec3 g110 = vec3(gx0.w,gy0.w,gz0.w);
179:   vec3 g001 = vec3(gx1.x,gy1.x,gz1.x);
180:   vec3 g101 = vec3(gx1.y,gy1.y,gz1.y);
181:   vec3 g011 = vec3(gx1.z,gy1.z,gz1.z);
182:   vec3 g111 = vec3(gx1.w,gy1.w,gz1.w);
183: 
184:   vec4 norm0 = taylorInvSqrt(vec4(dot(g000, g000), dot(g010, g010), dot(g100, g100), dot(g110, g110)));
185:   g000 *= norm0.x;
186:   g010 *= norm0.y;
187:   g100 *= norm0.z;
188:   g110 *= norm0.w;
189:   vec4 norm1 = taylorInvSqrt(vec4(dot(g001, g001), dot(g011, g011), dot(g101, g101), dot(g111, g111)));
190:   g001 *= norm1.x;
191:   g011 *= norm1.y;
192:   g101 *= norm1.z;
193:   g111 *= norm1.w;
194: 
195:   float n000 = dot(g000, Pf0);
196:   float n100 = dot(g100, vec3(Pf1.x, Pf0.yz));
197:   float n010 = dot(g010, vec3(Pf0.x, Pf1.y, Pf0.z));
198:   float n110 = dot(g110, vec3(Pf1.xy, Pf0.z));
199:   float n001 = dot(g001, vec3(Pf0.xy, Pf1.z));
200:   float n101 = dot(g101, vec3(Pf1.x, Pf0.y, Pf1.z));
201:   float n011 = dot(g011, vec3(Pf0.x, Pf1.yz));
202:   float n111 = dot(g111, Pf1);
203: 
204:   vec3 fade_xyz = fade(Pf0);
205:   vec4 n_z = mix(vec4(n000, n100, n010, n110), vec4(n001, n101, n011, n111), fade_xyz.z);
206:   vec2 n_yz = mix(n_z.xy, n_z.zw, fade_xyz.y);
207:   float n_xyz = mix(n_yz.x, n_yz.y, fade_xyz.x);
208:   return 2.2 * n_xyz;
209: }

211: vec3 saturation(vec3 rgb, float adjustment) {
212:     const vec3 W = vec3(0.2125, 0.7154, 0.0721);
213:     vec3 intensity = vec3(dot(rgb, W));
214:     return mix(intensity, rgb, adjustment);
215: }
216: 
217: float get_saturation(vec3 rgb)
218: {
219:     vec4 K = vec4(0.0, -1.0 / 3.0, 2.0 / 3.0, -1.0);
220:     vec4 p = mix(vec4(rgb.bg, K.wz), vec4(rgb.gb, K.xy), step(rgb.b, rgb.g));
221:     vec4 q = mix(vec4(p.xyw, rgb.r), vec4(rgb.r, p.yzx), step(p.x, rgb.r));
222: 
223:     float d = q.x - min(q.w, q.y);
224:     float e = 1.0e-10;
225:     return abs(6.0 * d + e);
226: }
227: 
228: // get saturation of a color in values between 0 and 1
229: float getSaturationMix(vec3 color) {
230:     float max = max(color.r, max(color.g, color.b));
231:     float min = min(color.r, min(color.g, color.b));
232:     return (max - min) / max;
233: }
234:     
235: vec3 rgb2hsv(vec3 c)
236: {
237:     vec4 K = vec4(0.0, -1.0 / 3.0, 2.0 / 3.0, -1.0);
238:     vec4 p = mix(vec4(c.bg, K.wz), vec4(c.gb, K.xy), step(c.b, c.g));
239:     vec4 q = mix(vec4(p.xyw, c.r), vec4(c.r, p.yzx), step(p.x, c.r));
240: 
241:     float d = q.x - min(q.w, q.y);
242:     float e = 1.0e-10;
243:     return vec3(abs(q.z + (q.w - q.y) / (6.0 * d + e)), d / (q.x + e), q.x);
244: }
245: 
246: vec3 hsv2rgb(vec3 c)
247: {
248:     vec4 K = vec4(1.0, 2.0 / 3.0, 1.0 / 3.0, 3.0);
249:     vec3 p = abs(fract(c.xxx + K.xyz) * 6.0 - K.www);
250:     return c.z * mix(K.xxx, clamp(p - K.xxx, 0.0, 1.0), c.y);
251: }
252: 
253: // Color related helper functions
254: vec3 blendColors(vec3 colorA, vec3 colorB, float weight) {
255:     return mix(colorA, colorB, weight);
256: }

258: precision highp float;
259: 
260: attribute vec3 position;
261: attribute vec3 normal;
262: attribute vec2 uv;
263: 
264: uniform mat4 modelViewMatrix;
265: uniform mat4 projectionMatrix;
266: 
267: // Uniforms injected by THREE previously:
268: // NONE that we don't define manually here.
269: 
270: void main() {
271:     vUv = uv;
272: 
273:     // SCROLLING LOGIC
274:     // Separate multipliers for wave, color, and flow offsets
275:     float waveOffset = -u_y_offset * u_y_offset_wave_multiplier;
276:     float colorOffset = -u_y_offset * u_y_offset_color_multiplier;
277:     float flowOffset = -u_y_offset * u_y_offset_flow_multiplier;
278: 
279:     // 1. DISPLACEMENT (WAVES)
280:     // We add waveOffset to Y to scroll the wave pattern
281:     v_displacement_amount = cnoise( vec3(
282:         u_wave_frequency_x * position.x + u_time,
283:         u_wave_frequency_y * (position.y + waveOffset) + u_time,
284:         u_time
285:     ));
286: 
287:     // 2. FLOW FIELD
288:     // Apply flow offset to scroll the flow field mask
289:     vec2 baseUv = vUv;
290:     baseUv.y += flowOffset / u_plane_height; // Scale to match wave speed
291:     vec2 flowUv = baseUv;
292: 
293:     if (u_flow_enabled > 0.5) {
294:         if (u_flow_ease > 0.0 || u_flow_distortion_a > 0.0) {
295:             vec2 ppp = -1.0 + 2.0 * baseUv;
296:             ppp += 0.1 * cos((1.5 * u_flow_scale) * ppp.yx + 1.1 * u_time + vec2(0.1, 1.1));
297:             ppp += 0.1 * cos((2.3 * u_flow_scale) * ppp.yx + 1.3 * u_time + vec2(3.2, 3.4));
298:             ppp += 0.1 * cos((2.2 * u_flow_scale) * ppp.yx + 1.7 * u_time + vec2(1.8, 5.2));
299:             ppp += u_flow_distortion_a * cos((u_flow_distortion_b * u_flow_scale) * ppp.yx + 1.4 * u_time + vec2(6.3, 3.9));
300: 
301:             float r = length(ppp);
302:             flowUv = mix(baseUv, vec2(baseUv.x * (1.0 - u_flow_ease) + r * u_flow_ease, baseUv.y), u_flow_ease);
303:         }
304:     }
305: 
306:     // Pass the standard flow UV to fragment shader (for mouse/texture)
307:     vFlowUv = flowUv;
308: 
309:     // 3. COLOR MIXING
310:     // We take the computed flow UVs and apply the color offset
311:     // Scale by plane height to match wave offset speed (world space vs UV space)
312:     vec3 color = u_colors[0].color;
313:     // ...
314:     vec2 adjustedUv = flowUv;
315:     adjustedUv.y += colorOffset / u_plane_height; // Scroll the color mixing pattern
316: 
317:     vec2 noise_cord = adjustedUv * u_color_pressure;
318:     const float minNoise = .0;
319:     const float maxNoise = .9;
320: 
321:     for (int i = 1; i < 6; i++) {
322:         if(i >= u_colors_count) break;
323:         if(u_colors[i].is_active > 0.5){
324:             float noiseFlow = (1. + float(i)) / 30.;
325:             float noiseSpeed = (1. + float(i)) * 0.11;
326:             float noiseSeed = 13. + float(i) * 7.;
327: 
328:             float noise = snoise(
329:                 vec3(
330:                     noise_cord.x * u_color_pressure.x + u_time * noiseFlow * 2.,
331:                     noise_cord.y * u_color_pressure.y,
332:                     u_time * noiseSpeed
333:                 ) + noiseSeed
334:             ) - (.1 * float(i)) + (.5 * u_color_blending);
335: 
336:             noise = clamp(minNoise, maxNoise + float(i) * 0.02, noise);
337:             color = mix(color, u_colors[i].color, smoothstep(0.0, u_color_blending, noise));
338:         }
339:     }
340: 
341:     v_color = color;
342: 
343:     // 4. VERTEX POSITION
344:     vec3 newPosition = position + normal * v_displacement_amount * u_wave_amplitude;
345:     gl_Position = projectionMatrix * modelViewMatrix * vec4(newPosition, 1.0);
346:     v_new_position = gl_Position;
347: }

122: // 3D Simplex Noise
123: float snoise(vec3 v) {
124:   const vec2  C = vec2(1.0/6.0, 1.0/3.0) ;
125:   const vec4  D = vec4(0.0, 0.5, 1.0, 2.0);
126: 
127:   // First corner
128:   vec3 i  = floor(v + dot(v, C.yyy) );
129:   vec3 x0 =   v - i + dot(i, C.xxx) ;
130: 
131:   // Other corners
132:   vec3 g = step(x0.yzx, x0.xyz);
133:   vec3 l = 1.0 - g;
134:   vec3 i1 = min( g.xyz, l.zxy );
135:   vec3 i2 = max( g.xyz, l.zxy );
136: 
137:   vec3 x1 = x0 - i1 + C.xxx;
138:   vec3 x2 = x0 - i2 + C.yyy;
139:   vec3 x3 = x0 - D.yyy;
140: 
141:   // Permutations
142:   vec4 p = permute( permute( permute(
143:             i.z + vec4(0.0, i1.z, i2.z, 1.0 ))
144:           + i.y + vec4(0.0, i1.y, i2.y, 1.0 ))
145:           + i.x + vec4(0.0, i1.x, i2.x, 1.0 ));
146: 
147:   // Gradients
148:   float n_ = 0.142857142857; // 1.0/7.0
149:   vec3  ns = n_ * D.wyz - D.xzx;
150: 
151:   vec4 j = p - 49.0 * floor(p * ns.z * ns.z);
152: 
153:   vec4 x_ = floor(j * ns.z);
154:   vec4 y_ = floor(j - 7.0 * x_ );
155: 
156:   vec4 x = x_ *ns.x + ns.yyyy;
157:   vec4 y = y_ *ns.x + ns.yyyy;
158:   vec4 h = 1.0 - abs(x) - abs(y);
159: 
160:   vec4 b0 = vec4( x.xy, y.xy );
161:   vec4 b1 = vec4( x.zw, y.zw );
162: 
163:   vec4 s0 = floor(b0)*2.0 + 1.0;
164:   vec4 s1 = floor(b1)*2.0 + 1.0;
165:   vec4 sh = -step(h, vec4(0.0));
166: 
167:   vec4 a0 = b0.xzyw + s0.xzyw*sh.xxyy ;
168:   vec4 a1 = b1.xzyw + s1.xzyw*sh.zzww ;
169: 
170:   vec3 p0 = vec3(a0.xy,h.x);
171:   vec3 p1 = vec3(a0.zw,h.y);
172:   vec3 p2 = vec3(a1.xy,h.z);
173:   vec3 p3 = vec3(a1.zw,h.w);
174: 
175:   // Normalise gradients
176:   vec4 norm = taylorInvSqrt(vec4(dot(p0,p0), dot(p1,p1), dot(p2, p2), dot(p3,p3)));
177:   p0 *= norm.x;
178:   p1 *= norm.y;
179:   p2 *= norm.z;
180:   p3 *= norm.w;
181: 
182:   // Mix final noise value
183:   vec4 m = max(0.6 - vec4(dot(x0,x0), dot(x1,x1), dot(x2,x2), dot(x3,x3)), 0.0);
184:   m = m * m;
185:   return 42.0 * dot( m*m, vec4( dot(p0,x0), dot(p1,x1),
186:                                 dot(p2,x2), dot(p3,x3) ) );
187: }
188: 
189: // Classic Perlin noise
190: float cnoise(vec3 P)
191: {
192:   vec3 Pi0 = floor(P); 
193:   vec3 Pi1 = Pi0 + vec3(1.0); 
194:   
195:   vec3 Pf0 = fract(P); 
196:   vec3 Pf1 = Pf0 - vec3(1.0); 
197:   vec4 ix = vec4(Pi0.x, Pi1.x, Pi0.x, Pi1.x);
198:   vec4 iy = vec4(Pi0.yy, Pi1.yy);
199:   vec4 iz0 = Pi0.zzzz;
200:   vec4 iz1 = Pi1.zzzz;
201: 
202:   vec4 ixy = permute(permute(ix) + iy);
203:   vec4 ixy0 = permute(ixy + iz0);
204:   vec4 ixy1 = permute(ixy + iz1);
205: 
206:   vec4 gx0 = ixy0 * (1.0 / 7.0);
207:   vec4 gy0 = fract(floor(gx0) * (1.0 / 7.0)) - 0.5;
208:   gx0 = fract(gx0);
209:   vec4 gz0 = vec4(0.5) - abs(gx0) - abs(gy0);
210:   vec4 sz0 = step(gz0, vec4(0.0));
211:   gx0 -= sz0 * (step(0.0, gx0) - 0.5);
212:   gy0 -= sz0 * (step(0.0, gy0) - 0.5);
213: 
214:   vec4 gx1 = ixy1 * (1.0 / 7.0);
215:   vec4 gy1 = fract(floor(gx1) * (1.0 / 7.0)) - 0.5;
216:   gx1 = fract(gx1);
217:   vec4 gz1 = vec4(0.5) - abs(gx1) - abs(gy1);
218:   vec4 sz1 = step(gz1, vec4(0.0));
219:   gx1 -= sz1 * (step(0.0, gx1) - 0.5);
220:   gy1 -= sz1 * (step(0.0, gy1) - 0.5);
221: 
222:   vec3 g000 = vec3(gx0.x,gy0.x,gz0.x);
223:   vec3 g100 = vec3(gx0.y,gy0.y,gz0.y);
224:   vec3 g010 = vec3(gx0.z,gy0.z,gz0.z);
225:   vec3 g110 = vec3(gx0.w,gy0.w,gz0.w);
226:   vec3 g001 = vec3(gx1.x,gy1.x,gz1.x);
227:   vec3 g101 = vec3(gx1.y,gy1.y,gz1.y);
228:   vec3 g011 = vec3(gx1.z,gy1.z,gz1.z);
229:   vec3 g111 = vec3(gx1.w,gy1.w,gz1.w);
230: 
231:   vec4 norm0 = taylorInvSqrt(vec4(dot(g000, g000), dot(g010, g010), dot(g100, g100), dot(g110, g110)));
232:   g000 *= norm0.x;
233:   g010 *= norm0.y;
234:   g100 *= norm0.z;
235:   g110 *= norm0.w;
236:   vec4 norm1 = taylorInvSqrt(vec4(dot(g001, g001), dot(g011, g011), dot(g101, g101), dot(g111, g111)));
237:   g001 *= norm1.x;
238:   g011 *= norm1.y;
239:   g101 *= norm1.z;
240:   g111 *= norm1.w;
241: 
242:   float n000 = dot(g000, Pf0);
243:   float n100 = dot(g100, vec3(Pf1.x, Pf0.yz));
244:   float n010 = dot(g010, vec3(Pf0.x, Pf1.y, Pf0.z));
245:   float n110 = dot(g110, vec3(Pf1.xy, Pf0.z));
246:   float n001 = dot(g001, vec3(Pf0.xy, Pf1.z));
247:   float n101 = dot(g101, vec3(Pf1.x, Pf0.y, Pf1.z));
248:   float n011 = dot(g011, vec3(Pf0.x, Pf1.yz));
249:   float n111 = dot(g111, Pf1);
250: 
251:   vec3 fade_xyz = fade(Pf0);
252:   vec4 n_z = mix(vec4(n000, n100, n010, n110), vec4(n001, n101, n011, n111), fade_xyz.z);
253:   vec2 n_yz = mix(n_z.xy, n_z.zw, fade_xyz.y);
254:   float n_xyz = mix(n_yz.x, n_yz.y, fade_xyz.x);
255:   return 2.2 * n_xyz;
256: }
257: 
258: 
259: float random(vec2 p) {
260:     return fract(sin(dot(p, vec2(12.9898,78.233))) * 43758.5453);
261: }
262: 
263: float fbm(vec3 x) {
264:     float value = 0.0;
265:     float amplitude = 0.5;
266:     float frequency = 1.0;
267:     for (int i = 0; i < 4; i++) {
268:         value += amplitude * snoise(x * frequency);
269:         frequency *= 2.0;
270:         amplitude *= 0.5;
271:     }
272:     return value;
273: }
274: 
275: void main() {
276:     // MOUSE DISTORTION
277:     vec2 finalUv = vFlowUv;
278:     
279:     if (u_mouse_distortion_strength > 0.0) {
280:         vec4 mouseColor = texture2D(u_mouse_texture, vUv);
281:         float mouseValue = mouseColor.r;
282:         
283:         if (mouseValue > 0.001) {
284:             float distortionAmount = mouseValue * u_mouse_distortion_strength;
285:             vec2 mouseDisp = vec2(distortionAmount, distortionAmount);
286:             finalUv -= mouseDisp;
287:         }
288:     }
289:     
290:     vec3 baseColor;
291: 
292:     if (u_enable_procedural_texture > 0.5) {
293:         // Calculate flow field distance for ease effect
294:         vec2 ppp = -1.0 + 2.0 * finalUv;
295:         ppp += 0.1 * cos((1.5 * u_flow_scale) * ppp.yx + 1.1 * u_time + vec2(0.1, 1.1));
296:         ppp += 0.1 * cos((2.3 * u_flow_scale) * ppp.yx + 1.3 * u_time + vec2(3.2, 3.4));
297:         ppp += 0.1 * cos((2.2 * u_flow_scale) * ppp.yx + 1.7 * u_time + vec2(1.8, 5.2));
298:         ppp += u_flow_distortion_a * cos((u_flow_distortion_b * u_flow_scale) * ppp.yx + 1.4 * u_time + vec2(6.3, 3.9));
299:         float r = length(ppp); // Flow distance
300:         
301:         // Ease blending: 0 = topographic (flow), 1 = image (UV)
302:         float vx = (finalUv.x * u_texture_ease) + (r * (1.0 - u_texture_ease));
303:         float vy = (finalUv.y * u_texture_ease) + (0.0 * (1.0 - u_texture_ease));
304:         vec2 texUv = vec2(vx, vy);
305: 
306:         // PARALLAX SCROLLING
307:         // We manually apply a smaller offset here to make the texture lag behind
308:         float parallaxFactor = 0.25; // 25% speed of the color mixing
309:         texUv.y -= (u_y_offset * u_y_offset_color_multiplier / u_plane_height) * parallaxFactor;
310: 
311:         texUv *= 1.5; // Tiling scale
312: 
313:         vec4 texSample = texture2D(u_procedural_texture, texUv);
314:         baseColor = texSample.rgb;
315:     } else {
316:         baseColor = v_color;
317:     }
318: 
319:     vec3 color = baseColor;
320: 
321:     // Post-processing
322:     color += pow(v_displacement_amount, 1.0) * u_highlights;
323:     color -= pow(1.0 - v_displacement_amount, 2.0) * u_shadows;
324:     color = saturation(color, 1.0 + u_saturation);
325:     color = color * u_brightness;
326: 
327:     // Grain
328:     vec2 noiseCoords = gl_FragCoord.xy / u_grain_scale;
329:     float grain = (u_grain_speed != 0.0) ? fbm(vec3(noiseCoords, u_time * u_grain_speed)) : fbm(vec3(noiseCoords, 0.0));
330: 
331:     grain = grain * 0.5 + 0.5;
332:     grain -= 0.5;
333:     grain = (grain > u_grain_sparsity) ? grain : 0.0;
334:     grain *= u_grain_intensity;
335: 
336:     color += vec3(grain);
337: 
338:     gl_FragColor = vec4(color, 1.0);
339: }
